{"parentUuid":"c6167e3b-8569-42ca-a0ca-3672045c0995","isSidechain":true,"promptId":"298b6713-e4c0-4e16-a467-4b545d28cfb4","agentId":"a4cf386f2f0d1d13e","type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01SSn1h9GnaKWqT43aUvMtLR","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→# ILLUSTRATOR.md — Integration MCP Illustrator\n     2→\n     3→> Moteur de rendu documentaire pour la plateforme pgView.\n     4→> MCP Illustrator est le composant de composition et d'export PDF pour tous les documents : devis, factures, brochures produits, communication.\n     5→\n     6→## Vision\n     7→\n     8→Deux mondes, un seul moteur de rendu :\n     9→\n    10→```\n    11→+------------------------------------------------------------------+\n    12→|  pgView (PostgreSQL)           |  MCP Illustrator                |\n    13→|  ============================  |  ============================== |\n    14→|  Affichage web interactif      |  Documents imprimables (PDF)    |\n    15→|  get_devis() -> HTML browser   |  Composition A4 -> PDF 300 DPI  |\n    16→|  Navigation, CRUD, workflow    |  Brochures, catalogues, com'    |\n    17→|  Temps reel, Alpine.js shell   |  Export pro, bleed, crop marks  |\n    18→+------------------------------------------------------------------+\n    19→                  |                              |\n    20→                  +--------- bridge -------------+\n    21→                  |                              |\n    22→          Donnees metier (PL/pgSQL)     Layout (Illustrator tools)\n    23→```\n    24→\n    25→pgView genere le HTML pour le navigateur. Illustrator compose les documents pour l'impression et l'export. Les donnees viennent du meme endroit : PostgreSQL.\n    26→\n    27→## Pourquoi Illustrator (pas un moteur HTML-to-PDF)\n    28→\n    29→Les moteurs HTML-to-PDF (Gotenberg, WeasyPrint, Puppeteer) convertissent du HTML en PDF. Ca marche, mais :\n    30→\n    31→| | HTML-to-PDF | Illustrator |\n    32→|---|------------|-------------|\n    33→| Controle layout | CSS @page, limites navigateur | Millimetrique, pixel-perfect |\n    34→| Typographie | Approximative (navigateur) | Precise (opentype.js, mesure glyphes) |\n    35→| Images | Contraintes CSS | Crop, zoom, filtres, ombres |\n    36→| Bleed / crop marks | Hack ou impossible | Natif, configurable |\n    37→| Brochures / com' | Hors scope | Use case principal |\n    38→| Template reutilisable | HTML + CSS a maintenir | Document clonable |\n    39→| UI de design | Aucune | Editeur web interactif |\n    40→| Clients potentiels | Aucun (c'est de l'infra) | Produit vendable separement |\n    41→\n    42→L'argument decisif : Illustrator sert **aussi** pour la communication (brochures, flyers, catalogues produit). Un moteur HTML-to-PDF ne fait que de la conversion — Illustrator est un outil de creation.\n    43→\n    44→## Architecture d'integration\n    45→\n    46→### Composants\n    47→\n    48→```\n    49→+---------------------------+        +---------------------------+\n    50→|  plpgsql-workbench        |        |  mcp-illustrator          |\n    51→|  (MCP server :3100)       |        |  (MCP server, stdio)      |\n    52→|                           |        |                           |\n    53→|  pg_query / pg_get        |        |  doc_new / doc_duplicate  |\n    54→|  -> donnees metier        |        |  batch_add / batch_update |\n    55→|                           |        |  export_pdf / snapshot    |\n    56→|  quote.devis_data(id)     |        |                           |\n    57→|  quote.facture_data(id)   |        |  Templates = documents    |\n    58→|  crm.client_data(id)      |        |  stockes dans SQLite      |\n    59→+---------------------------+        +---------------------------+\n    60→              |                                    |\n    61→              +------------- bridge ---------------+\n    62→              |                                    |\n    63→     +------------------+                          |\n    64→     |  Orchestrateur   |  (agent Claude, MCP tool, ou script)\n    65→     |  1. Query data   |\n    66→     |  2. Clone template|\n    67→     |  3. Fill data     |\n    68→     |  4. Export PDF    |\n    69→     +------------------+\n    70→```\n    71→\n    72→### Flux de generation\n    73→\n    74→```\n    75→1. QUERY     pg_query(\"SELECT quote.devis_data(42)\")\n    76→             -> { numero, date, client, lignes[], totaux, mentions[] }\n    77→\n    78→2. CLONE     doc_duplicate(\"tpl-devis-standard\")\n    79→             -> nouveau document \"DEV-2026-042\"\n    80→\n    81→3. FILL      batch_update([\n    82→               { name: \"numero\",     text: \"DEV-2026-042\" },\n    83→               { name: \"date\",       text: \"13 mars 2026\" },\n    84→               { name: \"client-nom\", text: \"Dupont SARL\" },\n    85→               ...\n    86→             ])\n    87→             + generation dynamique du tableau de lignes\n    88→\n    89→4. EXPORT    export_pdf({ format: \"A4\", home_print: true })\n    90→             -> PDF binaire\n    91→\n    92→5. CLEANUP   doc_delete(\"DEV-2026-042\")\n    93→             (ou archivage si besoin de re-generation)\n    94→```\n    95→\n    96→## Templates\n    97→\n    98→### Principe : template = document\n    99→\n   100→Pas de DSL, pas de Jinja, pas de moteur de substitution. Un template est un **document Illustrator standard** avec des elements nommes :\n   101→\n   102→```\n   103→tpl-devis-standard (A4 portrait)\n   104→├── logo              image    (x:15, y:15, w:40, h:20)\n   105→├── entreprise-nom    text     (x:15, y:40, \"ACME SARL\")\n   106→├── entreprise-addr   text     (x:15, y:48, \"12 rue des Lilas...\")\n   107→├── entreprise-siret  text     (x:15, y:62, \"SIRET: 123 456 789 00001\")\n   108→├── entreprise-tva    text     (x:15, y:67, \"TVA: FR12345678900\")\n   109→├── client-nom        text     (x:120, y:40, \"[client]\")\n   110→├── client-addr       text     (x:120, y:48, \"[adresse]\")\n   111→├── titre             text     (x:15, y:90, \"DEVIS DEV-XXXX-XXX\")\n   112→├── date              text     (x:160, y:90, \"[date]\")\n   113→├── validite          text     (x:160, y:96, \"Valide 30 jours\")\n   114→├── table-header      group    (y:110)\n   115→│   ├── col-desc      text     \"Description\"\n   116→│   ├── col-qte       text     \"Qte\"\n   117→│   ├── col-unite     text     \"Unite\"\n   118→│   ├── col-pu        text     \"P.U. HT\"\n   119→│   ├── col-tva       text     \"TVA\"\n   120→│   └── col-total     text     \"Total HT\"\n   121→├── table-lines       group    (y:118, genere dynamiquement)\n   122→├── total-ht          text     (x:160, y: calc, \"Total HT: 1 234,00\")\n   123→├── total-tva         text     (x:160, y: calc, \"TVA 20%:   246,80\")\n   124→├── total-ttc         text     (x:160, y: calc, \"Total TTC: 1 480,80\")\n   125→├── mentions          group    (y: bottom - 40)\n   126→│   ├── mention-1     text     \"Delai de paiement: 30 jours...\"\n   127→│   ├── mention-2     text     \"Penalites de retard: 10%...\"\n   128→│   └── mention-3     text     \"Indemnite forfaitaire: 40 EUR\"\n   129→├── watermark         text     (center, rotate:-45, opacity:0.08, \"BROUILLON\")\n   130→└── footer            group    (y: bottom - 10)\n   131→    ├── page-num      text     \"Page 1/1\"\n   132→    └── generation    text     \"Genere le 13/03/2026\"\n   133→```\n   134→\n   135→### Convention de nommage\n   136→\n   137→Les elements portent des noms semantiques que l'orchestrateur connait :\n   138→\n   139→| Prefixe | Contenu | Source |\n   140→|---------|---------|--------|\n   141→| `entreprise-*` | Coordonnees emetteur | `workbench.config('quote', ...)` |\n   142→| `client-*` | Coordonnees destinataire | `crm.client` |\n   143→| `titre`, `numero`, `date` | En-tete document | `quote.devis` / `quote.facture` |\n   144→| `table-header`, `table-lines` | Tableau des lignes | `quote.ligne` |\n   145→| `total-*` | Bloc totaux | Calcul `_total_ht/tva/ttc` |\n   146→| `mention-*` | Mentions legales | `quote.mention` |\n   147→| `watermark` | Filigrane conditionnel | Statut (BROUILLON, PAYE, ANNULE) |\n   148→| `footer` | Pied de page | Metadata generation |\n   149→\n   150→### Types de templates\n   151→\n   152→| Template | Format | Usage |\n   153→|----------|--------|-------|\n   154→| `tpl-devis-standard` | A4 portrait | Devis classique |\n   155→| `tpl-facture-standard` | A4 portrait | Facture |\n   156→| `tpl-bon-livraison` | A4 portrait | Bon de livraison |\n   157→| `tpl-avoir` | A4 portrait | Avoir / credit |\n   158→| `tpl-relance` | A4 portrait | Lettre de relance |\n   159→| `tpl-brochure-produit` | A4 paysage | Fiche produit catalogue |\n   160→| `tpl-catalogue-*` | A3/A4 | Catalogue multi-pages |\n   161→\n   162→### Personnalisation par tenant\n   163→\n   164→Les templates sont des documents Illustrator. Personnaliser = modifier le document :\n   165→\n   166→1. **Branding** — Remplacer le logo, les couleurs, les polices\n   167→2. **Layout** — Deplacer les blocs, redimensionner\n   168→3. **Contenu fixe** — Modifier les mentions, ajouter un slogan\n   169→4. **Nouveau template** — Dupliquer + modifier via l'UI web (localhost:3333)\n   170→\n   171→Pas de systeme de \"theme\" abstrait. Le template EST le design final — l'utilisateur ou l'agent le modifie directement.\n   172→\n   173→## Donnees metier\n   174→\n   175→### Fonctions d'extraction\n   176→\n   177→Chaque module expose une fonction `*_data()` qui retourne un JSONB structure, pret pour le remplissage :\n   178→\n   179→```sql\n   180→-- quote.devis_data(p_id int) RETURNS jsonb\n   181→{\n   182→  \"numero\": \"DEV-2026-042\",\n   183→  \"date\": \"2026-03-13\",\n   184→  \"validite\": \"2026-04-12\",\n   185→  \"statut\": \"brouillon\",\n   186→\n   187→  \"entreprise\": {\n   188→    \"nom\": \"ACME SARL\",\n   189→    \"adresse\": \"12 rue des Lilas, 39000 Lons-le-Saunier\",\n   190→    \"siret\": \"123 456 789 00001\",\n   191→    \"tva_intra\": \"FR12345678900\",\n   192→    \"telephone\": \"03 84 XX XX XX\",\n   193→    \"email\": \"contact@acme.fr\"\n   194→  },\n   195→\n   196→  \"client\": {\n   197→    \"nom\": \"Dupont SARL\",\n   198→    \"adresse\": \"5 avenue de la Gare, 25000 Besancon\",\n   199→    \"siret\": \"987 654 321 00001\"\n   200→  },\n   201→\n   202→  \"lignes\": [\n   203→    {\n   204→      \"description\": \"Conduit inox double paroi DN150\",\n   205→      \"quantite\": 6,\n   206→      \"unite\": \"ml\",\n   207→      \"prix_unitaire\": 89.50,\n   208→      \"tva_rate\": 20,\n   209→      \"total_ht\": 537.00\n   210→    },\n   211→    ...\n   212→  ],\n   213→\n   214→  \"totaux\": {\n   215→    \"total_ht\": 1234.00,\n   216→    \"total_tva\": 246.80,\n   217→    \"total_ttc\": 1480.80,\n   218→    \"tva_detail\": [\n   219→      { \"taux\": 20, \"base\": 1234.00, \"montant\": 246.80 }\n   220→    ]\n   221→  },\n   222→\n   223→  \"mentions\": [\n   224→    { \"label\": \"Delai de paiement\", \"texte\": \"30 jours a compter de...\" },\n   225→    { \"label\": \"Penalites de retard\", \"texte\": \"10% annuel...\" },\n   226→    { \"label\": \"Indemnite forfaitaire\", \"texte\": \"40 EUR...\" }\n   227→  ]\n   228→}\n   229→```\n   230→\n   231→### Coordonnees entreprise\n   232→\n   233→Stockees dans `workbench.config` (pas dans le template) :\n   234→\n   235→```sql\n   236→SELECT workbench.config('quote', 'entreprise_nom');\n   237→SELECT workbench.config('quote', 'entreprise_siret');\n   238→SELECT workbench.config('quote', 'entreprise_logo_path');\n   239→-- etc.\n   240→```\n   241→\n   242→Le template contient des placeholders. L'orchestrateur les remplace par les valeurs config au moment de la generation.\n   243→\n   244→## Generation dynamique du tableau\n   245→\n   246→Le tableau de lignes est le seul element qui varie en taille. L'orchestrateur doit :\n   247→\n   248→1. **Supprimer** le groupe `table-lines` du template (placeholder)\n   249→2. **Calculer** la position Y de depart (sous `table-header`)\n   250→3. **Ajouter** une ligne par element de `lignes[]` via `batch_add`\n   251→4. **Ajuster** les positions des blocs suivants (`total-*`, `mentions`, `footer`)\n   252→\n   253→```\n   254→Pour chaque ligne:\n   255→  add_text(name: \"line-N-desc\",  x: 15,  y: Y, text: ligne.description, fontSize: 8)\n   256→  add_text(name: \"line-N-qte\",  x: 120, y: Y, text: ligne.quantite,    fontSize: 8)\n   257→  add_text(name: \"line-N-pu\",   x: 145, y: Y, text: ligne.prix_unitaire, fontSize: 8)\n   258→  add_text(name: \"line-N-total\",x: 175, y: Y, text: ligne.total_ht,    fontSize: 8)\n   259→  Y += line_height (environ 5mm)\n   260→```\n   261→\n   262→### Multi-page\n   263→\n   264→Si le tableau depasse la zone imprimable :\n   265→\n   266→1. Detecter le depassement (Y > page_height - footer_height)\n   267→2. Couper le tableau, ajouter \"Suite page suivante\"\n   268→3. Creer un second document (page 2) avec le reste des lignes\n   269→4. Generer les PDFs separement, concatener (ou gerer via un futur `multi_page` dans Illustrator)\n   270→\n   271→**Evolution Illustrator necessaire** : support multi-page natif (aujourd'hui 1 doc = 1 page).\n   272→\n   273→## Watermarks et statuts\n   274→\n   275→| Statut | Watermark | Opacite | Rotation |\n   276→|--------|-----------|---------|----------|\n   277→| `brouillon` | BROUILLON | 0.08 | -45 deg |\n   278→| `envoye` / `envoyee` | _(aucun)_ | — | — |\n   279→| `accepte` | ACCEPTE | 0.05 | -45 deg |\n   280→| `refuse` | REFUSE | 0.08 | -45 deg |\n   281→| `payee` | PAYE | 0.05 | -45 deg |\n   282→| `annule` | ANNULE | 0.10 | -45 deg |\n   283→\n   284→L'orchestrateur met a jour l'element `watermark` (texte, opacite) ou le supprime selon le statut.\n   285→\n   286→## Use cases\n   287→\n   288→### 1. Documents commerciaux (automatique)\n   289→\n   290→```\n   291→Utilisateur clique \"Telecharger PDF\" sur un devis\n   292→  -> post_devis_pdf(id)\n   293→  -> orchestrateur query data + clone template + fill + export\n   294→  -> PDF retourne au navigateur\n   295→```\n   296→\n   297→Entierement automatise. L'utilisateur ne voit jamais Illustrator.\n   298→\n   299→### 2. Brochure produit (semi-automatique)\n   300→\n   301→```\n   302→Agent recoit : \"Fais-moi une fiche produit pour le conduit DN150\"\n   303→  -> Query donnees catalogue (stock, prix, specs)\n   304→  -> doc_duplicate(\"tpl-brochure-produit\")\n   305→  -> Compose : photo produit, specs techniques, prix, argumentaire\n   306→  -> Ajuste le layout (positionnement, couleurs)\n   307→  -> export_pdf -> PDF\n   308→```\n   309→\n   310→L'agent utilise les MCP tools directement. L'utilisateur peut ensuite affiner via l'UI.\n   311→\n   312→### 3. Communication (creatif)\n   313→\n   314→```\n   315→Agent recoit : \"Cree une affiche pour les portes ouvertes du 15 avril\"\n   316→  -> doc_new format A3 portrait\n   317→  -> Compose librement (titre, photo, programme, logo, QR code)\n   318→  -> snapshot -> preview PNG\n   319→  -> Iterations avec l'utilisateur\n   320→  -> export_pdf -> PDF pro pour imprimeur\n   321→```\n   322→\n   323→Aucun template pre-defini. Composition libre pilotee par l'agent.\n   324→\n   325→## Factur-X (e-invoicing 2026-2027)\n   326→\n   327→La facturation electronique impose le format **Factur-X** : un PDF/A-3 avec XML CII embarque.\n   328→\n   329→### Pipeline\n   330→\n   331→```\n   332→1. export_pdf(facture)           -> PDF standard\n   333→2. quote.facture_xml_cii(id)     -> XML CII (genere par PL/pgSQL via xmlelement/xmlforest)\n   334→3. facturx_embed(pdf, xml)       -> PDF/A-3 avec XML attache\n   335→```\n   336→\n   337→L'etape 3 necessite un outil d'embedding (Python `factur-x` lib par Akretion, ou Ghostscript). Peut etre un service Docker sidecar minimaliste.\n   338→\n   339→### XML CII\n   340→\n   341→PL/pgSQL genere le XML nativement :\n   342→\n   343→```sql\n   344→SELECT xmlelement(\n   345→  name \"rsm:CrossIndustryInvoice\",\n   346→  xmlattributes('urn:un:unece:uncefact:data:standard:...' AS \"xmlns:rsm\"),\n   347→  xmlelement(name \"rsm:ExchangedDocumentContext\", ...),\n   348→  xmlelement(name \"rsm:ExchangedDocument\",\n   349→    xmlelement(name \"ram:ID\", f.numero),\n   350→    xmlelement(name \"ram:TypeCode\", '380'),\n   351→    xmlelement(name \"ram:IssueDateTime\", ...)\n   352→  ),\n   353→  ...\n   354→)\n   355→FROM quote.facture f WHERE f.id = p_id;\n   356→```\n   357→\n   358→Zero dependance externe pour la generation XML. Seul l'embedding dans le PDF necessite un outil tiers.\n   359→\n   360→## Evolutions Illustrator necessaires\n   361→\n   362→| Evolution | Priorite | Description |\n   363→|-----------|----------|-------------|\n   364→| **Multi-page** | Haute | Support natif de documents multi-pages (factures longues, catalogues) |\n   365→| **Tableaux** | Haute | Element `table` natif avec colonnes, lignes, auto-layout |\n   366→| **Variables** | Moyenne | Systeme `{{nom}}` optionnel pour pre-remplissage sans batch_update |\n   367→| **QR Code** | Moyenne | Generation QR natif (paiement, lien web, Factur-X) |\n   368→| **PDF/A** | Moyenne | Export PDF/A-3 natif (pre-requis Factur-X sans outil tiers) |\n   369→| **Fusion PDF** | Basse | Concatenation multi-pages en un seul fichier |\n   370→| **Styles** | Basse | Presets de styles reutilisables (police + taille + couleur = \"body\") |\n   371→\n   372→## Positionnement commercial\n   373→\n   374→```\n   375→+-----------------------------------------------+\n   376→|  Produit                | Cible               |\n   377→|======================== |=====================|\n   378→|  ERP pgView             | TPE/PME (gestion)   |\n   379→|  + Illustrator integre  | Documents pro       |\n   380→|  Illustrator standalone | Agences, artisans   |\n   381→|                         | (com', brochures)   |\n   382→+-----------------------------------------------+\n   383→```\n   384→\n   385→Illustrator a une double vie :\n   386→\n   387→1. **Composant integre** — Le moteur PDF de l'ERP. L'utilisateur final ne le voit pas, il clique \"Telecharger PDF\" et ca marche.\n   388→2. **Produit autonome** — Un outil de creation documentaire pilote par IA. Les clients l'achetent pour faire leurs brochures, flyers, catalogues.\n   389→\n   390→Cette dualite est un avantage strategique : le meme code sert deux marches.\n   391→"}]},"uuid":"63b42eea-29d2-4bc5-b2ed-46c078271699","timestamp":"2026-03-13T22:01:15.153Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"c6167e3b-8569-42ca-a0ca-3672045c0995","userType":"external","cwd":"/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench","sessionId":"32666746-590f-450a-9377-59546bb90632","version":"2.1.75","gitBranch":"main","slug":"quizzical-honking-yao"}

146→\n   147→export async function handleTool(name: string, args: any) {\n   148→  switch (name) {\n   149→    // ---- Documents ----\n   150→    case \"doc_new\": {\n   151→      const fmt =   225→      if (getDocuments().has(args.name)) return txt(`Document \"${args.name}\" already exists`);\n   226→      const clone = structuredClone(sourceDoc);\n   227→      clone.name = args.name;\n   228→      // Reassign element IDs (recursive for groups)\n   229→      clone.nextId = reassignIds(clone.elements, 1);\n   230→      getDocuments().set(clone.name, clone);\n   231→      setActiveDoc(clone.name);\n   232→      saveDocToDisk(clone);\n   233→      bus.emit(\"document:created\", { name: clone.name });\n   234→      bus.emit(\"toast\", { text: `Document \"${sourceName}\" \"${args.name}\" already exists`);\n   242→      const oldName = d.name;\n   243→      getStore().deleteDoc(oldName);\n   244→      getDocuments().delete(oldName);\n   245→      d.name = args.name;\n format: fmt,\n   296→        orientation: orient,\n   297→        w, h,\n   298→        bg: args.background || d.canvas.bg,\n   299→      };\n   300→      bus.emit(\"canvas:changed\", {});\n   301→ \"backward\"];\n   526→      if (!validActions.includes(action)) return txt(`Invalid action: ${action}`);\n   527→      const el = parent.splice(i, 1)[0];\n   528→      switch (action) {\n   529→        case \"to_front\":\n   530→          parent.push(el);\n   531→          break;\n   532→        case \"to_back\":\n   533→          parent.unshift(el);\n   534→          break;\n   535→        case \"forward\":\n   536→          parent.splice(Math.min(i + 1, parent.length), 0, el);\n   537→          break;\n   538→        case \"backward\":\n   539→          parent.splice(Math.max(i - 1, 0), 0, el);\n   540→          break;\n   541→      }\n   542→      bus.emit(\"element:reordered\", { id: args.id, action });\n   543→      return txt(`Reordered ${args.id} → ${action}`);\n   544→    }\n [];\n   765→        return txt(`Dispatched ${args.event_type} → phase: ${resp.phase}, selectedIds: [${ids.join(\",\")}]`);\n   766→      } catch (e: any) {\n   767→        return txt(`dispatch_event 783→          const ago = ((now - e.ts) / 1000).toFixed(1);\n   784→          const blocked = e.blocked ? \"  [BLOCKED]\" : \"\";\n   785→          const detail = e.detail ? `  ${e.detail}` : \"\";\n 82→  const sw = 0.15;     // stroke-width in mm\n    83→\n    84→  // In SVG coordinates, trim box starts at (0,0) and content area is at (bleed, bleed)\n    85→  // But our SVG viewBox starts at (-bleed, -bleed)\n    86→  // So trim edges are at x=0, x=contentW, y=0, y=contentH\n    87→  const tl = 0, tr = contentW, tt = 0, tb = contentH;\n    88→\n    89→  const lines = [\n    90→    // 24→function hex(c: string): string { return c.replace(\"#\", \"\"); }\n    25→\n    26→/** Detect the document's gold accent color (v3=#B07A2B, v4=#D4A43C) */\n    27→function detectGold(elements: FlatEl[]): string {\n    28→  for (const el of elements) {\n    29→    if (el.type === \"rect\" && el.fill && /^#[BbDd][04][7Aa][42][2Cc3][BbCc]$/.test(el.fill)) {\n    30→      return hex(el.fill);\n    31→    }\n    32→    if (el.type === \"text\" && el.fill && /^#[BbDd][04][7Aa][42][2Cc3][BbCc]$/.test(el.fill)) {\n    33→      return hex(el.fill);\n    34→    }\n    35→  }\n    36→  return 42→  fontWeight?: string; fontStyle?: string; fill?: string;\n    43→  textAnchor?: string; maxWidth?: number;\n    44→  path?: string; width?: number; height?: number;\n    45→  [key: string]: any;\n    46→}\n    47→\n    48→/** Flatten all elements (recurse into groups), sorted by y position */\n    49→function flattenElements(elements: Element[]): FlatEl[] {\n    50→  const result: FlatEl[] = */\n    63→function goldRule(gold: string): Paragraph {\n    64→  return new Paragraph({\n    65→    spacing: { before: 160, after: 160 },\n    66→    border: { bottom: { style: BorderStyle.SINGLE, size: 4, color: gold, space: 1 } },\n    67→    children: [],\n    68→  });\n    69→}\n    70→\n    71→/** Build an axe table cell */\n    72→function axeCell(gold: string, num: string, title: string, {\n   103→  return new TableCell({\n   104→    width: { size: 3, type: WidthType.PERCENTAGE },\n   105→    borders: {\n   106→      top: { style: BorderStyle.NONE, size: 0, color: WHITE },\n   107→ === 0 && i.width === 210);\n   128→  if (heroImg?.path) {\n   129→    try {\n   130→      const imgData = readFileSync(join(ASSETS_DIR, heroImg.path));\n   131→      const aspect = (heroImg.height || 142→  }\n   143→\n   144→  // ==================== Categorize texts by position ====================\n   145→  // Find the programme title to split hero/intro from axes\n   146→  const progTitle = texts.find(t =>\n   147→    t.text?.includes(\"PROGRAMME\") && t.textAnchor === \"middle\"\n   148→  );\n   149→  const progY = progTitle ? ?? 0;\n   165→    return y > heroH + 5 && y < progY - 2 && t !== progTitle;\n   166→  });\n   167→\n   168→  // Axe texts: between programme title and footer\n   169→  const axeTexts = texts.filter(t children: [new TextRun({ text: txt, bold: isBold, italics: isItalic, size: 20, color: GRIS, font: \"Source Sans 3\" })],\n   228→      }));\n   229→    }\n   230→  }\n   231→\n   232→  // 337→  for (const t of footerTexts) {\n   338→    const txt = (t.text || \"\").trim();\n   339→    if (!txt) continue;\n   340→    const isBold = t.fontWeight === \"bold\" || t.fontWeight === {"parentUuid":"9b985a7b-7844-4f1e-aee2-2d4e67e104de","isSidechain":true,"agentId":"a4cf386f2f0d1d13e","type":"progress","data":{"type":"hook_progress","hookEvent":"PostToolUse","hookName":"PostToolUse:Read","command":"callback"},"parentToolUseID":"toolu_01YRDo51Aai2gytTKgqwVVXS","toolUseID":"toolu_01YRDo51Aai2gytTKgqwVVXS","timestamp":"2026-03-13T22:02:22.230Z","uuid":"8f3742d3-42b2-4e31-8bba-44f1d562feb4","userType":"external","cwd":"/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench","sessionId":"32666746-590f-450a-9377-59546bb90632","version":"2.1.75","gitBranch":"main","slug":"quizzical-honking-yao"}
{"parentUuid":"d810da26-e64b-45aa-81a9-b4bfa6b98328","isSidechain":true,"promptId":"a3a75031-e3a5-435c-b2fc-52cc34158646","agentId":"a4cf386f2f0d1d13e","type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01YRDo51Aai2gytTKgqwVVXS","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→// ============================================================\n     2→// POSITIONING — relative placement, align, distribute\n     3→// ============================================================\n     4→\n     5→import type { Document, Element, Canvas, BBox } from \"./types.js\";\n     6→import { bbox } from \"./layout.js\";\n     7→import { measureTextWidth, wrapText } from \"./fonts.js\";\n     8→import { findInTree } from \"./tree.js\";\n     9→\n    10→/** Find element by ID or name (recursive) */\n    11→function findRef(doc: Document, idOrName: string): Element | undefined {\n    12→  return findInTree(doc.elements, idOrName);\n    13→}\n    14→\n    15→// ---- Relative positioning for add_* ----\n    16→\n    17→interface RelativeArgs {\n    18→  below?: string;\n    19→  above?: string;\n    20→  right_of?: string;\n    21→  left_of?: string;\n    22→  gap?: number;\n    23→  center_h?: boolean;\n    24→  center_v?: boolean;\n    25→}\n    26→\n    27→interface ResolvedPos {\n    28→  x?: number;\n    29→  y?: number;\n    30→  x1?: number;\n    31→  y1?: number;\n    32→  x2?: number;\n    33→  y2?: number;\n    34→}\n    35→\n    36→/**\n    37→ * Compute text bounding box dimensions for an element being created.\n    38→ * Returns { w, h } in mm.\n    39→ */\n    40→function textDims(args: any): { w: number; h: number } {\n    41→  const fontSize = args.fontSize ?? 8;\n    42→  const fontFamily = args.fontFamily ?? \"Libre Baskerville\";\n    43→  const fontWeight = args.fontWeight ?? \"bold\";\n    44→  const fontStyle = args.fontStyle ?? \"normal\";\n    45→  const maxWidth = args.maxWidth ?? null;\n    46→  const lines = wrapText(args.text, maxWidth, fontSize, fontFamily, fontWeight, fontStyle);\n    47→  const tw = Math.max(\n    48→    ...lines.map((l) => measureTextWidth(l, fontSize, fontFamily, fontWeight, fontStyle)),\n    49→  );\n    50→  const th = fontSize * lines.length * 1.3;\n    51→  return { w: tw, h: th };\n    52→}\n    53→\n    54→/**\n    55→ * Resolve relative positioning params into concrete x/y values.\n    56→ * Returns resolved coordinates to merge into the element args.\n    57→ * Throws on errors (missing reference, no coordinates resolved).\n    58→ */\n    59→export function resolvePosition(\n    60→  doc: Document,\n    61→  type: string,\n    62→  args: any,\n    63→): ResolvedPos {\n    64→  const rel: RelativeArgs = {\n    65→    below: args.below,\n    66→    above: args.above,\n    67→    right_of: args.right_of,\n    68→    left_of: args.left_of,\n    69→    gap: args.gap ?? 0,\n    70→    center_h: args.center_h,\n    71→    center_v: args.center_v,\n    72→  };\n    73→\n    74→  const gap = rel.gap!;\n    75→  const canvas = doc.canvas;\n    76→  const result: ResolvedPos = {};\n    77→  const isLine = type === \"line\";\n    78→  const hasRelative = rel.below || rel.above || rel.right_of || rel.left_of;\n    79→\n    80→  // Get reference element bbox if relative positioning is used\n    81→  let refBox: BBox | undefined;\n    82→  let refEl: Element | undefined;\n    83→  const refName = rel.below || rel.above || rel.right_of || rel.left_of;\n    84→  if (refName) {\n    85→    refEl = findRef(doc, refName);\n    86→    if (!refEl) throw new Error(`Reference element not found: \"${refName}\"`);\n    87→    refBox = bbox(refEl);\n    88→  }\n    89→\n    90→  // ---- Vertical axis (below / above) ----\n    91→  if (rel.below && refBox) {\n    92→    const targetY = refBox.y + refBox.h + gap;\n    93→    if (isLine) {\n    94→      // offset y1/y2\n    95→      result.y1 = targetY + (args.y1 ?? 0);\n    96→      result.y2 = targetY + (args.y2 ?? 0);\n    97→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n    98→      // text y is baseline: add fontSize*0.85\n    99→      result.y = targetY + (args.fontSize ?? 8) * 0.85;\n   100→    } else {\n   101→      result.y = targetY;\n   102→    }\n   103→  }\n   104→\n   105→  if (rel.above && refBox) {\n   106→    if (isLine) {\n   107→      const lineH = Math.abs((args.y2 ?? 0) - (args.y1 ?? 0));\n   108→      const targetY = refBox.y - gap - lineH;\n   109→      result.y1 = targetY + (args.y1 ?? 0);\n   110→      result.y2 = targetY + (args.y2 ?? 0);\n   111→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n   112→      // text: y is baseline, place so bottom of text aligns above ref\n   113→      result.y = refBox.y - gap;\n   114→    } else {\n   115→      // rect/image: place so bottom edge is at ref.y - gap\n   116→      const h = args.height ?? 0;\n   117→      result.y = refBox.y - gap - h;\n   118→    }\n   119→  }\n   120→\n   121→  // ---- Horizontal axis (right_of / left_of) ----\n   122→  if (rel.right_of && refBox) {\n   123→    const targetX = refBox.x + refBox.w + gap;\n   124→    if (isLine) {\n   125→      result.x1 = targetX + (args.x1 ?? 0);\n   126→      result.x2 = targetX + (args.x2 ?? 0);\n   127→    } else {\n   128→      result.x = targetX;\n   129→    }\n   130→  }\n   131→\n   132→  if (rel.left_of && refBox) {\n   133→    if (isLine) {\n   134→      const lineW = Math.abs((args.x2 ?? 0) - (args.x1 ?? 0));\n   135→      const targetX = refBox.x - gap - lineW;\n   136→      result.x1 = targetX + (args.x1 ?? 0);\n   137→      result.x2 = targetX + (args.x2 ?? 0);\n   138→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n   139→      // text width depends on anchor\n   140→      const dims = textDims(args);\n   141→      const anchor = args.textAnchor ?? \"start\";\n   142→      if (anchor === \"end\") {\n   143→        result.x = refBox.x - gap;\n   144→      } else if (anchor === \"middle\") {\n   145→        result.x = refBox.x - gap - dims.w / 2;\n   146→      } else {\n   147→        result.x = refBox.x - gap - dims.w;\n   148→      }\n   149→    } else {\n   150→      const w = args.width ?? 0;\n   151→      result.x = refBox.x - gap - w;\n   152→    }\n   153→  }\n   154→\n   155→  // ---- Inherit orthogonal axis from reference ----\n   156→  if (refBox && refEl) {\n   157→    if ((rel.below || rel.above) && result.x == null && args.x == null && !rel.center_h && !isLine) {\n   158→      // Inherit x from reference element\n   159→      if (type === \"text\" && \"x\" in refEl) {\n   160→        result.x = (refEl as any).x;\n   161→      } else if (\"x\" in refEl) {\n   162→        result.x = (refEl as any).x;\n   163→      } else {\n   164→        result.x = refBox.x;\n   165→      }\n   166→    }\n   167→    if ((rel.right_of || rel.left_of) && result.y == null && args.y == null && !rel.center_v && !isLine) {\n   168→      // Inherit y from reference element\n   169→      if (\"y\" in refEl) {\n   170→        result.y = (refEl as any).y;\n   171→      } else {\n   172→        result.y = refBox.y;\n   173→      }\n   174→    }\n   175→    // For lines: inherit orthogonal axis as offset\n   176→    if (isLine && (rel.below || rel.above) && result.x1 == null && args.x1 == null) {\n   177→      if (\"x1\" in refEl) {\n   178→        result.x1 = (refEl as any).x1;\n   179→        result.x2 = (refEl as any).x2;\n   180→      } else {\n   181→        result.x1 = refBox.x;\n   182→        result.x2 = refBox.x + refBox.w;\n   183→      }\n   184→    }\n   185→    if (isLine && (rel.right_of || rel.left_of) && result.y1 == null && args.y1 == null) {\n   186→      if (\"y1\" in refEl) {\n   187→        result.y1 = (refEl as any).y1;\n   188→        result.y2 = (refEl as any).y2;\n   189→      } else {\n   190→        result.y1 = refBox.y;\n   191→        result.y2 = refBox.y + refBox.h;\n   192→      }\n   193→    }\n   194→  }\n   195→\n   196→  // ---- Canvas centering ----\n   197→  if (rel.center_h) {\n   198→    if (isLine) {\n   199→      const x1 = result.x1 ?? args.x1 ?? 0;\n   200→      const x2 = result.x2 ?? args.x2 ?? 0;\n   201→      const lineW = Math.abs(x2 - x1);\n   202→      const offset = (canvas.w - lineW) / 2 - Math.min(x1, x2);\n   203→      result.x1 = x1 + offset;\n   204→      result.x2 = x2 + offset;\n   205→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n   206→      const anchor = args.textAnchor ?? \"start\";\n   207→      if (anchor === \"middle\") {\n   208→        result.x = canvas.w / 2;\n   209→      } else if (anchor === \"end\") {\n   210→        const dims = textDims(args);\n   211→        result.x = canvas.w / 2 + dims.w / 2;\n   212→      } else {\n   213→        const dims = textDims(args);\n   214→        result.x = (canvas.w - dims.w) / 2;\n   215→      }\n   216→    } else {\n   217→      const w = args.width ?? 0;\n   218→      result.x = (canvas.w - w) / 2;\n   219→    }\n   220→  }\n   221→\n   222→  if (rel.center_v) {\n   223→    if (isLine) {\n   224→      const y1 = result.y1 ?? args.y1 ?? 0;\n   225→      const y2 = result.y2 ?? args.y2 ?? 0;\n   226→      const lineH = Math.abs(y2 - y1);\n   227→      const offset = (canvas.h - lineH) / 2 - Math.min(y1, y2);\n   228→      result.y1 = y1 + offset;\n   229→      result.y2 = y2 + offset;\n   230→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n   231→      const dims = textDims(args);\n   232→      result.y = (canvas.h - dims.h) / 2 + (args.fontSize ?? 8) * 0.85;\n   233→    } else {\n   234→      const h = args.height ?? 0;\n   235→      result.y = (canvas.h - h) / 2;\n   236→    }\n   237→  }\n   238→\n   239→  // ---- Explicit args always win ----\n   240→  // For non-line types, if x or y was explicitly provided and no relative override happened,\n   241→  // keep them. The caller should merge result over args, so we only set result if computed.\n   242→  // For lines: explicit x1/y1/x2/y2 are kept unless overridden above.\n   243→\n   244→  return result;\n   245→}\n   246→\n   247→/**\n   248→ * Check if relative positioning args are present\n   249→ */\n   250→export function hasRelativeArgs(args: any): boolean {\n   251→  return !!(args.below || args.above || args.right_of || args.left_of || args.center_h || args.center_v);\n   252→}\n   253→\n   254→// ---- Align ----\n   255→\n   256→type AlignAxis = \"left\" | \"center_h\" | \"right\" | \"top\" | \"center_v\" | \"bottom\";\n   257→\n   258→interface AlignArgs {\n   259→  ids: string[];\n   260→  axis: AlignAxis;\n   261→}\n   262→\n   263→interface ElementDelta {\n   264→  id: string;\n   265→  props: Record<string, number>;\n   266→}\n   267→\n   268→export function computeAlign(doc: Document, args: AlignArgs): ElementDelta[] {\n   269→  const elements = args.ids.map((idOrName) => {\n   270→    const el = findRef(doc, idOrName);\n   271→    if (!el) throw new Error(`Element not found: \"${idOrName}\"`);\n   272→    return el;\n   273→  });\n   274→\n   275→  const boxes = elements.map((el) => ({ el, box: bbox(el) }));\n   276→  const deltas: ElementDelta[] = [];\n   277→\n   278→  switch (args.axis) {\n   279→    case \"left\": {\n   280→      const target = Math.min(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.x));\n   281→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   282→        const dx = target - box.x;\n   283→        if (Math.abs(dx) < 0.01) continue;\n   284→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, 0));\n   285→      }\n   286→      break;\n   287→    }\n   288→    case \"right\": {\n   289→      const target = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.x + b.box.w));\n   290→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   291→        const dx = target - (box.x + box.w);\n   292→        if (Math.abs(dx) < 0.01) continue;\n   293→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, 0));\n   294→      }\n   295→      break;\n   296→    }\n   297→    case \"center_h\": {\n   298→      const minX = Math.min(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.x));\n   299→      const maxR = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.x + b.box.w));\n   300→      const center = (minX + maxR) / 2;\n   301→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   302→        const elCenter = box.x + box.w / 2;\n   303→        const dx = center - elCenter;\n   304→        if (Math.abs(dx) < 0.01) continue;\n   305→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, 0));\n   306→      }\n   307→      break;\n   308→    }\n   309→    case \"top\": {\n   310→      const target = Math.min(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.y));\n   311→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   312→        const dy = target - box.y;\n   313→        if (Math.abs(dy) < 0.01) continue;\n   314→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, 0, dy));\n   315→      }\n   316→      break;\n   317→    }\n   318→    case \"bottom\": {\n   319→      const target = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.y + b.box.h));\n   320→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   321→        const dy = target - (box.y + box.h);\n   322→        if (Math.abs(dy) < 0.01) continue;\n   323→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, 0, dy));\n   324→      }\n   325→      break;\n   326→    }\n   327→    case \"center_v\": {\n   328→      const minY = Math.min(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.y));\n   329→      const maxB = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.y + b.box.h));\n   330→      const center = (minY + maxB) / 2;\n   331→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   332→        const elCenter = box.y + box.h / 2;\n   333→        const dy = center - elCenter;\n   334→        if (Math.abs(dy) < 0.01) continue;\n   335→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, 0, dy));\n   336→      }\n   337→      break;\n   338→    }\n   339→  }\n   340→\n   341→  return deltas;\n   342→}\n   343→\n   344→// ---- Distribute ----\n   345→\n   346→interface DistributeArgs {\n   347→  ids: string[];\n   348→  axis?: \"x\" | \"y\";\n   349→  gap?: number;\n   350→  grid?: {\n   351→    cols: number;\n   352→    col_gap: number;\n   353→    row_gap: number;\n   354→    start_x?: number;\n   355→    start_y?: number;\n   356→  };\n   357→}\n   358→\n   359→export function computeDistribute(doc: Document, args: DistributeArgs): ElementDelta[] {\n   360→  const elements = args.ids.map((idOrName) => {\n   361→    const el = findRef(doc, idOrName);\n   362→    if (!el) throw new Error(`Element not found: \"${idOrName}\"`);\n   363→    return el;\n   364→  });\n   365→\n   366→  if (args.grid) {\n   367→    return distributeGrid(elements, args.grid);\n   368→  }\n   369→\n   370→  const axis = args.axis ?? \"y\";\n   371→  const boxes = elements.map((el) => ({ el, box: bbox(el) }));\n   372→\n   373→  // Sort by position on axis\n   374→  boxes.sort((a, b) =>\n   375→    axis === \"x\" ? a.box.x - b.box.x : a.box.y - b.box.y,\n   376→  );\n   377→\n   378→  const n = boxes.length;\n   379→  if (n < 2) return [];\n   380→\n   381→  const deltas: ElementDelta[] = [];\n   382→\n   383→  if (axis === \"x\") {\n   384→    const totalSize = boxes.reduce((s, b) => s + b.box.w, 0);\n   385→    let gap: number;\n   386→    let startX: number;\n   387→\n   388→    if (args.gap != null) {\n   389→      gap = args.gap;\n   390→      startX = boxes[0].box.x;\n   391→    } else {\n   392→      const extent = boxes[n - 1].box.x + boxes[n - 1].box.w - boxes[0].box.x;\n   393→      gap = (extent - totalSize) / (n - 1);\n   394→      startX = boxes[0].box.x;\n   395→    }\n   396→\n   397→    let currentX = startX;\n   398→    for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   399→      const dx = currentX - box.x;\n   400→      if (Math.abs(dx) >= 0.01) {\n   401→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, 0));\n   402→      }\n   403→      currentX += box.w + gap;\n   404→    }\n   405→  } else {\n   406→    const totalSize = boxes.reduce((s, b) => s + b.box.h, 0);\n   407→    let gap: number;\n   408→    let startY: number;\n   409→\n   410→    if (args.gap != null) {\n   411→      gap = args.gap;\n   412→      startY = boxes[0].box.y;\n   413→    } else {\n   414→      const extent = boxes[n - 1].box.y + boxes[n - 1].box.h - boxes[0].box.y;\n   415→      gap = (extent - totalSize) / (n - 1);\n   416→      startY = boxes[0].box.y;\n   417→    }\n   418→\n   419→    let currentY = startY;\n   420→    for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   421→      const dy = currentY - box.y;\n   422→      if (Math.abs(dy) >= 0.01) {\n   423→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, 0, dy));\n   424→      }\n   425→      currentY += box.h + gap;\n   426→    }\n   427→  }\n   428→\n   429→  return deltas;\n   430→}\n   431→\n   432→function distributeGrid(\n   433→  elements: Element[],\n   434→  grid: { cols: number; col_gap: number; row_gap: number; start_x?: number; start_y?: number },\n   435→): ElementDelta[] {\n   436→  const boxes = elements.map((el) => ({ el, box: bbox(el) }));\n   437→  const startX = grid.start_x ?? boxes[0].box.x;\n   438→  const startY = grid.start_y ?? boxes[0].box.y;\n   439→\n   440→  // Compute max dimensions per column and row for uniform grid\n   441→  const cols = grid.cols;\n   442→  const maxColW = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.w));\n   443→  const maxRowH = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.h));\n   444→\n   445→  const deltas: ElementDelta[] = [];\n   446→\n   447→  for (let i = 0; i < boxes.length; i++) {\n   448→    const col = i % cols;\n   449→    const row = Math.floor(i / cols);\n   450→    const targetX = startX + col * (maxColW + grid.col_gap);\n   451→    const targetY = startY + row * (maxRowH + grid.row_gap);\n   452→\n   453→    const { el, box } = boxes[i];\n   454→    const dx = targetX - box.x;\n   455→    const dy = targetY - box.y;\n   456→\n   457→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= 0.01 || Math.abs(dy) >= 0.01) {\n   458→      deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, dy));\n   459→    }\n   460→  }\n   461→\n   462→  return deltas;\n   463→}\n   464→\n   465→// ---- Shared: apply delta to raw coordinates ----\n   466→\n   467→function applyDelta(el: Element, dx: number, dy: number): ElementDelta {\n   468→  const props: Record<string, number> = {};\n   469→  if (el.type === \"line\") {\n   470→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= 0.01) {\n   471→      props.x1 = r(el.x1 + dx);\n   472→      props.x2 = r(el.x2 + dx);\n   473→    }\n   474→    if (Math.abs(dy) >= 0.01) {\n   475→      props.y1 = r(el.y1 + dy);\n   476→      props.y2 = r(el.y2 + dy);\n   477→    }\n   478→  } else {\n   479→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= 0.01) props.x = r((el as any).x + dx);\n   480→    if (Math.abs(dy) >= 0.01) props.y = r((el as any).y + dy);\n   481→  }\n   482→  return { id: el.id, props };\n   483→}\n   484→\n   485→function r(v: number): number {\n   486→  return Math.round(v * 10) / 10;\n   487→}\n   488→"}]},"uuid":"0d642383-4643-43e0-8cbf-86f4fd3f4314","timestamp":"2026-03-13T22:02:22.229Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"d810da26-e64b-45aa-81a9-b4bfa6b98328","userType":"external","cwd":"/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench","sessionId":"32666746-590f-450a-9377-59546bb90632","version":"2.1.75","gitBranch":"main","slug":"quizzical-honking-yao"}

{"parentUuid":"5e7bcff1-c635-4fe7-9995-05b9bbffa2a8","isSidechain":true,"promptId":"a3a75031-e3a5-435c-b2fc-52cc34158646","agentId":"a4cf386f2f0d1d13e","type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01A3F9cxhmbdHzJixirths53","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→// ============================================================\n     2→// LAYOUT — check_layout: bbox, overlaps, bleed, spacing\n     3→// ============================================================\n     4→\n     5→import type { Document, Element, GroupElement, BBox } from \"./types.js\";\n     6→import { wrapText, measureTextWidth } from \"./fonts.js\";\n     7→import { flattenLeaves } from \"./tree.js\";\n     8→\n     9→export function bbox(el: Element): BBox {\n    10→  switch (el.type) {\n    11→    case \"rect\":\n    12→    case \"image\":\n    13→      return { x: el.x, y: el.y, w: el.width, h: el.height };\n    14→    case \"line\": {\n    15→      const x = Math.min(el.x1, el.x2), y = Math.min(el.y1, el.y2);\n    16→      return { x, y, w: Math.abs(el.x2 - el.x1) || 0.5, h: Math.abs(el.y2 - el.y1) || 0.5 };\n    17→    }\n    18→    case \"text\": {\n    19→      const lines = el.maxWidth\n    20→        ? wrapText(el.text, el.maxWidth, el.fontSize, el.fontFamily, el.fontWeight, el.fontStyle)\n    21→        : el.text.split(\"\\n\");\n    22→      const tw = el.maxWidth\n    23→        ? el.fontSize * 0.85;\n    30→      return { x: tx, y: ty, w: tw, h: th };\n    31→    }\n    32→    case \"group\": {\n    33→      const children = (el as GroupElement).children;\n    34→      if (!children.length) return { x: 0, y: 0, w: 0, h: 0 };\n    35→      let minX = Infinity, minY = Infinity, maxX = -Infinity, maxY = -Infinity;\n    36→      for (const child of children) {\n    37→        const cb = bbox(child);\n    38→        minX = Math.min(minX, cb.x);\n    39→        minY = Math.min(minY, cb.y);\n    40→        maxX = Math.max(maxX, cb.x + cb.w);\n    41→        maxY = Math.max(maxY, cb.y + cb.h);\n    42→      }\n    43→      return { x: minX, y: minY, w: maxX - minX, h: maxY - minY };\n    44→    }\n    45→    default:\n    46→      return { x: 0, y: 0, w: 0, h: 0 };\n    47→  }\n    48→}\n    49→\n    50→export interface ColorWarning {\n    51→  id: string;\n    52→  type: string;\n    53→  property: string;\n    54→  value: string;\n    55→  reason: string;\n    56→}\n    57→\n    58→export interface LayoutReport {\n    59→  structuralLayers: string[];\n    60→  overlaps: any[];\n    61→  outOfBounds: any[];\n    62→  bleedZone: any[];\n    63→  spacingGroups: any[];\n    64→  colorWarnings: ColorWarning[];\n    65→}\n    66→\n    67→export function checkLayout(\n    68→  d: Document,\n    69→  bleed: number,\n    70→  spaceTol: number,\n    71→  sizeTol: number,\n    72→): LayoutReport {\n    73→  const { w: cW, h: cH } = d.canvas;\n    74→\n    75→  const leaves = flattenLeaves(d.elements);\n    76→  const boxes = leaves.map((el) => ({ id: el.id, type: el.type, bbox: bbox(el), el }));\n    77→\n    78→  // Structural layer detection\n    79→  const canvasArea = cW * cH;\n    80→  const isStructural = (b: typeof boxes[0]) => {\n    81→    const area = b.bbox.w * b.bbox.h;\n    82→    if (area > canvasArea * 0.5) return true;\n    83→    if (b.type === \"rect\" && (b.el.opacity ?? 1) < 1 && (b.bbox.w >= cW * 0.95 || b.bbox.h >= cH * 0.95)) return true;\n    84→    return false;\n    85→  };\n    86→  const structuralIds = new Set(boxes.filter(isStructural).map((b) => b.id));\n    87→\n    88→  // 1. Pairwise overlaps (skip structural layers)\n    89→  const overlaps: any[] = [];\n    90→  for (let i = 0; i < boxes.length; i++) {\n    91→    for (let j = i + 1; j < boxes.length; j++) {\n    92→      if (structuralIds.has(boxes[i].id) || structuralIds.has(boxes[j].id)) continue;\n    93→      const a = boxes[i].bbox, b = boxes[j].bbox;\n    94→      const ix = Math.max(a.x, b.x);\n    95→      const iy = Math.max(a.y, b.y);\n    96→      const ix2 = Math.min(a.x + a.w, b.x + b.w);\n    97→      const iy2 = Math.min(a.y + a.h, b.y + b.h);\n    98→      if (ix < ix2 && iy < iy2) {\n    99→        const iw = Math.round((ix2 - ix) * 10) / 10;\n   100→        const ih = Math.round((iy2 - iy) * 10) / 10;\n   101→        overlaps.push({\n   102→          a: boxes[i].id,\n   103→          b: boxes[j].id,\n   104→          a_type: boxes[i].type,\n   105→          b_type: boxes[j].type,\n   106→          intersection: { x: Math.round(ix * 10) / 10, y: Math.round(iy * 10) / 10, w: iw, h: ih },\n   107→          area_mm2: Math.round(iw * ih * 10) / 10,\n   108→        });\n   109→      }\n   110→    }\n   111→  }\n   112→\n   113→  // 2. Out of bounds\n   114→  const outOfBounds: any[] = [];\n   115→  for (const b of boxes) {\n   116→    const { x, y, w, h } = b.bbox;\n   117→    const sides: any[] = [];\n   118→    if (x < 0) sides.push({ side: \"left\", overflow_mm: Math.round(-x * 10) / 10 });\n   119→    if (y < 0) sides.push({ side: \"top\", overflow_mm: Math.round(-y * 10) / 10 });\n   120→    if (x + w > cW) sides.push({ side: \"right\", overflow_mm: Math.round((x + w - cW) * 10) / 10 });\n   121→    if (y + h > cH) sides.push({ side: \"bottom\", overflow_mm: Math.round((y + h - cH) * 10) / 10 });\n   122→    for (const s of sides) outOfBounds.push({ id: b.id, ...s });\n   123→  }\n   124→\n   125→  // 3. Bleed zone\n   126→  const bleedZone: any[] = [];\n   127→  for (const b of boxes) {\n   128→    const { x, y, w, h } = b.bbox;\n   129→    if (w >= cW * 0.95 && h >= cH * 0.95) continue;\n   130→    const sides: any[] = [];\n   131→    if (x > 0 && x < bleed) sides.push({ side: \"left\", distance_mm: Math.round(x * 10) / 10 });\n   132→    if (y > 0 && y < bleed) sides.push({ side: \"top\", distance_mm: Math.round(y * 10) / 10 });\n   133→    if (x + w < cW && cW - (x + w) < bleed) sides.push({ side: \"right\", distance_mm: Math.round((cW - x - w) * 10) / 10 });\n   134→    if (y + h < cH && cH - (y + h) < bleed) sides.push({ side: \"bottom\", distance_mm: Math.round((cH - y - h) * 10) / 10 });\n   135→    for (const s of sides) bleedZone.push({ id: b.id, ...s });\n   136→  }\n   137→\n   138→  // 4. Spacing groups\n   139→  const spacingGroups: any[] = [];\n   140→  const sizeKey = (b: typeof boxes[0]) => `${b.type}_${Math.round(b.bbox.w / sizeTol) * sizeTol}_${Math.round(b.bbox.h / sizeTol) * sizeTol}`;\n   141→  const groups = new Map<string, typeof boxes>();\n   142→  for (const b of boxes) {\n   143→    const k = sizeKey(b);\n   144→    if (!groups.has(k)) groups.set(k, []);\n   145→    groups.get(k)!.push(b);\n   146→  }\n   147→  for (const [, members] of groups) {\n   148→    if (members.length < 3) continue;\n   149→    const ys = members.map((m) => m.bbox.y);\n   150→    const ySpread = Math.max(...ys) - Math.min(...ys);\n   151→    const xs = members.map((m) => m.bbox.x);\n   152→    const xSpread = Math.max(...xs) - Math.min(...xs);\n   153→\n   154→    if (xSpread > ySpread) {\n   155→      const sorted = [...members].sort((a, b) => a.bbox.x - b.bbox.x);\n   156→      const gaps: number[] = [];\n   157→      for (let i = 1; i < sorted.length; i++) {\n   174→        gaps.push(Math.round((sorted[i].bbox.y - sorted[i - 1].bbox.y - sorted[i - 1].bbox.h) * 10) / 10);\n   175→      }\n   176→      const avgGap = gaps.reduce((s, g) => s + g, 0) / gaps.length;\n   177→      const uniform = gaps.every((g) => Math.abs(g - avgGap) <= spaceTol);\n   178→      spacingGroups.push({\n   179→        ids: sorted.map((m) => m.id),\n   180→        type: members[0].type,\n   181→        axis: \"vertical\",\n   182→        gaps_mm: gaps,\n   183→        avg_gap_mm: Math.round(avgGap * 10) / 10,\n   184→        uniform,\n   185→      });\n   186→    }\n   187→  }\n   188→\n   189→  // 5. CMYK color warnings\n   190→  const colorWarnings: ColorWarning[] = [];\n   191→  for (const b of boxes) {\n   192→    const el = b.el;\n   193→    const colorProps: [string, string | undefined][] = [\n   194→      [\"fill\", (el as any).fill],\n   195→      [\"stroke\", (el as any).stroke],\n   196→      [\"borderColor\", (el as any).borderColor],\n   197→      [\"shadowColor\", (el as any).shadowColor],\n   198→    ];\n   199→    for (const [prop, val] of colorProps) {\n   200→      if (!val || val === \"none\") continue;\n   201→      if (/^rgba?\\s*\\(/.test(val) && /,\\s*[\\d.]+\\s*\\)$/.test(val) && !/,\\s*1\\s*\\)$/.test(val)) {\n   202→        colorWarnings.push({ id: b.id, type: b.type, property: prop, value: val, reason: \"Transparence (alpha) non supportée en CMJN\" });\n   203→      }\n   204→      if (/^hsla?\\s*\\(/.test(val)) {\n   205→        colorWarnings.push({ id: b.id, type: b.type, property: prop, value: val, reason: \"Couleur HSL — convertir en hex pour l'impression\" });\n   206→      }\n   207→      if (val === \"#000000\" || val === \"#000\" || val.toLowerCase() === \"black\") {\n   208→        colorWarnings.push({ id: b.id, type: b.type, property: prop, value: val, reason: \"Noir pur — utiliser un noir riche (ex: #1C1C1C) pour l'impression\" });\n   209→      }\n   210→      // Detect highly saturated colors likely out of CMYK gamut\n   211→      const hex = parseHex(val);\n   212→      if (hex) {\n   213→        const [r, g, _b] = hex;\n   214→        const max = Math.max(r, g, _b);\n   215→        const min = Math.min(r, g, _b);\n   216→        if (max === 255 && min === 0 && (r === 0 || g === 0 || _b === 0)) {\n   217→          colorWarnings.push({ id: b.id, type: b.type, property: prop, value: val, reason: \"Couleur très saturée — hors gamut CMJN probable\" });\n   218→        }\n   219→      }\n   220→    }\n   221→  }\n   222→\n   223→  return { structuralLayers: [...structuralIds], overlaps, outOfBounds, bleedZone, spacingGroups, colorWarnings };\n   224→}\n   225→\n   226→function parseHex(val: string): [number, number, number] | null {\n   227→  const m3 = val.match(/^#([0-9a-f])([0-9a-f])([0-9a-f])$/i);\n   228→  if (m3) return [parseInt(m3[1] + m3[1], 16), parseInt(m3[2] + m3[2], 16), parseInt(m3[3] + m3[3], 16)];\n   229→  const m6 = 48→export function measureTextWidth(text: string, fontSize: number, fontFamily?: string, fontWeight?: string, fontStyle?: string): number {\n    49→  const font = getFont(fontFamily, fontWeight, fontStyle);\n    50→  if (!font) return text.length * fontSize * 0.55;\n    51→  return font.getAdvanceWidth(text, fontSize);\n    52→}\n    53→\n    54→export function wrapText(text: string, maxWidth: number | null, fontSize: number, fontFamily?: string, fontWeight?: string, fontStyle?: string): string[] {\n    55→  if (!maxWidth) return text.split(\"\\n\");\n    56→  const paragraphs = text.split(\"\\n\");\n    57→  const lines: string[] = [];\n    58→  for (const para of paragraphs) {\n    59→    const words = para.split(/\\s+/).filter(Boolean);\n    60→    if (!words.length) { el.fontSize * 0.85, w: tw, h: th };\n    40→  }\n    41→  return { x: (el as any).x, y: (el as any).y, w: (el as any).width || 0, h: (el as any).height || 0 };\n    42→}\n    43→\n    44→/** Pre-compute snap points once at drag start (#11) */\n    45→export function collectSnapTargets(\n    46→  elements: Element[],\n    47→  excludeIds: Set<string>,\n    48→  canvas: { w: number; h: number },\n    49→): SnapTargets {\n    50→  const xSnaps = [0, canvas.w / 2, canvas.w];\n    51→  const ySnaps = [0, canvas.h / 2, canvas.h];\n    52→  for (const el of flattenLeaves(elements)) {\n    53→    if (excludeIds.has(el.id)) continue;\n    54→    const b = elBbox(el);\n    55→    xSnaps.push(b.x, b.x + b.w / 2, b.x + b.w);\n    56→    ySnaps.push(b.y, b.y + b.h / 2, b.y + b.h);\n    57→  }\n    58→  return { xSnaps, ySnaps };\n    59→}\n    60→\n    61→export function computeSnap(\n    62→  dragBbox: BBox,\n    63→  targets: SnapTargets,\n    64→): SnapResult {\n    65→  const { xSnaps, ySnaps } = targets;\n    66→\n    67→  const dLeft = dragBbox.x;\n    68→  const dCenterX = dragBbox.x + dragBbox.w / 2;\n    69→  const dRight = dragBbox.x + dragBbox.w;\n    70→  const dTop = dragBbox.y;\n    71→  const dCenterY = dragBbox.y + dragBbox.h / 2;\n    72→  const dBottom = dragBbox.y + dragBbox.h;\n    73→\n    74→  let bestDx = Infinity;\n    75→  let snapX = dragBbox.x;\n    76→  let guideX: number | null = null;\n    77→\n    78→  for (const sx of xSnaps) {\n    79→    for (const anchor of [dLeft, dCenterX, dRight]) {\n    80→      const dist = Math.abs(anchor - sx);\n    81→      if (dist < THRESHOLD && dist < Math.abs(bestDx)) {\n    82→        bestDx = anchor - sx;\n    83→        snapX = dragBbox.x - bestDx;\n    84→        guideX = sx;\n    85→      }\n    86→    }\n    87→  }\n    88→\n    89→  let bestDy = Infinity;\n    90→  let snapY = dragBbox.y;\n    91→  let guideY: number | null = null;\n    92→\n    93→  for (const sy of ySnaps) {\n    94→    for (const anchor of [dTop, dCenterY, dBottom]) {\n    95→      const dist = Math.abs(anchor - sy);\n    96→      if (dist < THRESHOLD && dist < Math.abs(bestDy)) {\n    97→        bestDy = anchor - sy;\n    98→        snapY = dragBbox.y - bestDy;\n    99→        guideY = sy;\n   100→      }\n   101→    }\n   102→  }\n   103→\n   104→  const guides: Guide[] = [];\n   105→  if (guideX !== null) guides.push({ axis: \"v\", pos: guideX });\n   106→  if (guideY !== null) guides.push({ axis: \"h\", pos: guideY });\n   107→\n   108→  return { x: snapX, y: snapY, guides };\n   109→}\n   110→"}]},"uuid":"5704e66d-5bd5-4a17-b224-06a0e126d06d","timestamp":"2026-03-13T22:02:55.906Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"442b6294-b214-4e0e-a914-b2766f56d348","userType":"external","cwd":"/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench","sessionId":"32666746-590f-450a-9377-59546bb90632","version":"2.1.75","gitBranch":"main","slug":"quizzical-honking-yao"}

dragStartY;\n   147→\n   148→    // Convert pixel drag to crop delta (0-1)\n   149→    const zoom = draft.cropZoom || 1;\n   150→    const baseScale = Math.max(frameW / natW, frameH / natH);\n   151→ parseFloat(frame.style.width) / frameW;\n   156→    const dcx = excessW > 0 ? -(dxPx / previewScale) / excessW : 0;\n   157→    const dcy = excessH > 0 ? -(dyPx / previewScale) / excessH : 0;\n   158→\n   159→    draft.cropX = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, dragStartCropX + dcx));\n   160→    draft.cropY = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, dragStartCropY + dcy));\n   161→    updatePreview();\n   162→  };\n   163→\n   164→  const onUp = () => { isDragging = false; };\n   165→  document.addEventListener('mousemove', onMove);\n   166→  document.addEventListener('mouseup', onUp);\n   167→  cleanupListeners = = previewImg.parentElement!;\n   190→  const pxW = parseFloat(frame.style.width);\n   191→  const pxH = parseFloat(frame.style.height);\n   192→  const scaleRatio = pxW / frameW; // preview pixels per mm\n   193→\n   194→  if (draft.objectFit === 'cover') {\n   195→    const zoom = draft.cropZoom || 1;\n   196→    const baseScale = Math.max(frameW / natW, frameH / natH);\n   197→    const imgScale const imgY = -(imgH - pxH) * draft.cropY;\n   202→\n   203→    previewImg.style.width = imgW + 'px';\n   204→    previewImg.style.height = imgH + 'px';\n   205→    previewImg.style.left = imgX + 'px';\n   206→    previewImg.style.top = imgY + 'px';\n   207→  } else if (draft.objectFit === 'contain') {\n   208→    const fitScale = Math.min(pxW / natW, pxH / natH);\n   209→    const w = natW * \"./types.js\";\n     8→import type { AppEvent } from \"./events.js\";\n     9→\n    10→function docReducer(slice: DocumentSlice, event: AppEvent): DocumentSlice {\n    11→  switch (event.type) {\n    12→    case \"SERVER_STATE\":\n    13→      // Skip if same doc reference (dedup)\n    14→      if (slice.currentDoc === event.doc && slice.docList === event.docList) return slice;\n    15→ case \"TOGGLE_SHOW_BLEED\":\n    48→      return { ...slice, showBleed: !slice.showBleed };\n    49→    case \"TOGGLE_SNAP\":\n    50→      return { ...slice, snapEnabled: !slice.snapEnabled };\n (event.type) {\n    62→    case \"DRAG_START\":\n    63→      return { ...slice, snapGuides: [] };\n    64→    case \"DRAG_MOVE\":\n    65→      return { ...slice, snapGuides: event.snapGuides };\n    66→    case \"DRAG_END\":\n    67→      if (slice.snapGuides.length === 0) return slice;\n    68→      return { ...slice, snapGuides: [] };\n    69→    case \"SET_ZOOM_LEVEL\":\n    70→      return { ...slice, zoomLevel: event.level };\n    71→    default:\n    72→      return slice;\n    73→  }\n    74→}\n    75→\n    76→function refsReducer(slice: RefsSlice, event: AppEvent): RefsSlice {\n 89→function phaseReducer(phase: AppPhase, event: AppEvent, ui: UISlice): AppPhase {\n    90→  switch (event.type) {\n    91→    case \"PHASE_TRANSITION\":\n    92→      return event.to;\n    93→    case \"SERVER_STATE\":\n    94→      if (event.doc && (phase === \"loading\" || phase === \"loading_doc\")) {\n    95→        return ui.selectedIds.length > 0 ? \"selected\" : \"idle\";\n    96→      }\n    97→      if (!event.doc) return \"loading\";\n    98→      return phase;\n    99→    case \"SELECT_ELEMENT\":\n   100→      if (phase === \"dragging\") return phase; // guard: no phase change during drag\n   101→      return ui.selectedIds.length > 0 ? \"selected\" : \"idle\";\n   102→    case \"DRAG_START\":\n   103→      return \"dragging\";\n   104→    case \"DRAG_END\":\n   105→      return \"selected\";\n   106→    default:\n   107→      return phase;\n   108→  }\n   109→}\n   110→\n   111→export function rootReducer(state: AppState, event: AppEvent): AppState {\n   112→  const doc = docReducer(state.doc, event);\n   113→  const ui = uiReducer(state.ui, event);\n   114→  const ephemeral = ephemeralReducer(state.ephemeral, event);\n   115→  const refs = refsReducer(state.refs, event);\n   116→  const phase = phaseReducer(state.phase, event, ui);\n   117→\n   118→  // Return same reference if nothing changed (enables === checks in subscribers)\n   119→  if (\n   120→    doc === state.doc &&\n   121→    ui === state.ui &&\n   122→    ephemeral === state.ephemeral &&\n   123→    refs === state.refs &&\n   124→    phase === state.phase\n   125→  )
