Path is relative to assets/ (e.g. \\\"photo.jpg\\\") or absolute. Supports relative positioning: below/above/right_of/left_of + gap, center_h/center_v. x/y are optional when using relative placement.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `path` (string, required) — Filename in assets/ or absolute path\n  - `width` (number, required) — Width in mm\n  - `height` (number, required) — Height in mm\n  - `name` (string, optional)\n  - `x` (number, optional) — optional if using relative positioning\n  - `y` (number, optional) — optional if using relative positioning\n  - `preserveAspectRatio` (string, optional) — `\"xMidYMid slice\"` (cover) or `\"xMidYMid meet\"` (contain), default `\"xMidYMid slice\"`\n  - `opacity` (number, optional) — 0-1, default `1`\n  - `rotation` (number, optional) — Degrees, default `0`\n  - `brightness` (number, optional) — 50-150%, default `100`\n  - `contrast` (number, optional) — 50-150%, default `100`\n  - `grayscale` (number, optional) — 0-100, default `0`\n  - `clipX` (number, optional) — Crop start X in mm\n  - `clipY` (number, optional) — Crop start Y in mm\n  - `clipW` (number, optional) — Crop width in mm\n  - `clipH` (number, optional) — Crop height in mm\n  - `borderWidth` (number, optional) — Border width in mm, default `0`\n  - `borderColor` (string, optional) — Border color hex, default `\"#000\"`\n  - `borderRadius` (number, optional) — Border radius in mm, default `0`\n  - `shadowX` (number, optional) — Shadow offset X in mm, default `0`\n  - `shadowY` (number, optional) — Shadow offset Y in mm, default `0`\n  - `shadowBlur` (number, optional) — Shadow blur radius in mm, default `0`\n  - `shadowColor` (string, optional) — Shadow color, default `\"rgba(0,0,0,0.4)\"`\n  - Relative positioning props\n- Annotations: none\n\n**`add_rect`**\n- Description: \"Add a rectangle. Supports relative positioning.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `width` (number, required)\n  - `height` (number, required)\n  - `name` (string, optional)\n  - `x` (number, optional)\n  - `y` (number, optional)\n  - `fill` (string, optional) — Hex or `\"none\"`, default `\"#000000\"`\n  - `stroke` (string, optional) — default `\"none\"`\n  - `strokeWidth` (number, optional) — default `0`\n  - `rx` (number, optional) — Border radius in mm, default `0`\n  - `opacity` (number, optional) — default `1`\n  - `rotation` (number, optional) — default `0`\n  - Relative positioning props\n- Annotations: none\n\n**`add_line`**\n- Description: \"Add a line. Supports relative positioning. When using relative placement, x1/y1/x2/y2 are treated as offsets from the resolved position.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `x1` (number, required)\n  - `y1` (number, required)\n  - `x2` (number, required)\n  - `y2` (number, required)\n  - `name` (string, optional)\n  - `stroke` (string, optional) — default `\"#000000\"`\n  - `strokeWidth` (number, optional) — default `0.5`\n  - `opacity` (number, optional) — default `1`\n  - `rotation` (number, optional) — default `0`\n  - Relative positioning props\n- Annotations: none\n\n**Shared `relativeProps` object** (included in add_text, add_image, add_rect, add_line):\n- `below` (string, optional) — Place below this element (ID or name). Inherits x unless x or center_h is set.\n- `above` (string, optional) — Place above this element (ID or name). Inherits x unless x or center_h is set.\n- `right_of` (string, optional) — Place right of this element (ID or name). Inherits y unless y or center_v is set.\n- `left_of` (string, optional) — Place left of this element (ID or name). Inherits y unless y or center_v is set.\n- `gap` (number, optional) — Spacing in mm from reference element, default `0`. Used with below/above/right_of/left_of.\n- `center_h` (boolean, optional) — Center horizontally on canvas.\n- `center_v` (boolean, optional) — Center vertically on canvas.\n- `group` (string, optional) — Add element inside this group (ID or name). If omitted, adds to top level.\n\n---\n\n### Category: Element Mutation\n\n**`update_element`**\n- Description: \"Update properties of an existing element. Pass only changed properties.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `id` (string, required) — Element ID or name\n  - `props` (object, required) — Properties to update (any element property)\n- Annotations: none\n\n**`batch_update`**\n- Description: \"Update multiple elements at once. Pass an array of {id, props} objects. Single broadcast after all updates.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `updates` (array, required) — Array of `{ id: string, props: object }` objects\n- Annotations: none\n\n**`batch_add`**\n- Description: \"Add multiple elements in one call. Each item needs a 'type' field (text/image/rect/line) plus the same properties as the individual add_* tools. Returns all created IDs. Elements are added in order.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `elements` (array, required) — Array of objects each with `type: \"text\" | \"image\" | \"rect\" | \"line\"` plus type-specific properties\n- Annotations: none\n\n**`element_duplicate`**\n- Description: \"Duplicate an element with an offset. Works on groups (deep clone with recursive ID reassignment). Returns the new element ID.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `id_or_name` (string, required) — Element ID or name to duplicate\n  - `offset_x` (number, optional) — Horizontal offset in mm, default `5`\n  - `offset_y` (number, optional) — Vertical offset in mm, default `5`\n- Annotations: none\n\n**`delete_element`**\n- Description: \"Remove an element by ID or name. If the element is a group, all children are deleted too. Works on elements inside groups.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `id` (string, required) — Element ID or name\n- Annotations: destructiveHint\n\n**`reorder_element`**\n- Description: \"Change z-order.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `id` (string, required)\n  - `action` (string, required) — enum: `\"to_front\" | \"to_back\" | \"forward\" | \"backward\"`\n- Annotations: none\n\n---\n\n### Category: Alignment and Distribution\n\n**`align`**\n- Description: \"Align multiple elements along an axis. Moves elements to match edges or centers. Uses element bounding boxes for accurate alignment.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `ids` (string[], required) — Element IDs or names (minimum 2)\n  - `axis` (string, required) — enum: `\"left\" | \"center_h\" | \"right\" | \"top\" | \"center_v\" | \"bottom\"`\n- Annotations: none\n\n**`distribute`**\n- Description: \"Distribute elements with equal spacing. Supports linear distribution on x/y axis or grid layout. Elements are sorted by current position before distributing.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `ids` (string[], required) — Element IDs or names (minimum 2)\n  - `axis` (string, optional) — enum: `\"x\" | \"y\"`. Omit if using grid.\n  - `gap` (number, optional) — Fixed gap in mm between elements. If omitted, distributes uniformly across current extent.\n  - `grid` (object, optional):\n    - `cols` (number, required) — Number of columns\n    - `col_gap` (number, required) — Horizontal gap between columns in mm\n    - `row_gap` (number, required) — Vertical gap between rows in mm\n    - `start_x` (number, optional) — Grid start X in mm (default: position of first element)\n    - `start_y` (number, optional) — Grid start Y in mm (default: position of first element)\n- Annotations: none\n\n---\n\n### Category: State and Inspection\n\n**`get_state`**\n- Description: \"Get current document state. Default: compact text table (token-efficient). Use format='full' for complete JSON.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `format` (string, optional) — enum: `\"compact\" | \"full\"`, default `\"compact\"`\n- Annotations: readOnlyHint\n\n**`measure_text`**\n- Description: \"Measure text dimensions before placing. Returns line count, total width, and height in mm. Use to plan layout without trial-and-error.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `text` (string, required)\n  - `fontSize` (number, required)\n  - `fontFamily` (string, optional) — enum: `\"Libre Baskerville\" | \"Source Sans 3\"`\n  - `fontWeight` (string, optional) — enum: `\"normal\" | \"bold\" | \"300\" | \"600\" | \"700\"`\n  - `fontStyle` (string, optional) — enum: `\"normal\" | \"italic\"`\n  - `maxWidth` (number, optional) — Max width in mm for word-wrap\n- Annotations: readOnlyHint\n\n**`clear_canvas`**\n- Description: \"Remove all elements. Keeps canvas and doc name.\"\n- Parameters: none\n- Annotations: destructiveHint\n\n---\n\n### Category: Export\n\n**`snapshot`**\n- Description: \"Take a PNG snapshot of the current document to visually inspect layout and positioning. Returns an image.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `width` (number, optional) — Output width in pixels, default `1200`\n- Annotations: readOnlyHint\n\n**`export_svg`**\n- Description: \"Export current document as standalone SVG markup for print.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `embed_images` (boolean, optional) — Embed images as base64, default `true`. Set `false` for lighter SVG with file references.\n- Annotations: readOnlyHint\n\n**`export_pdf`**\n- Description: \"Export current document as vector PDF via headless Chrome. Use home_print=true for home/office printers (scales content within safe margins, no bleed/crop marks).\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `bleed_mm` (number, optional) — Bleed zone in mm, default `3`. Ignored if home_print.\n  - `crop_marks` (boolean, optional) — Include crop marks, default `true`. Ignored if home_print.\n  - `dpi` (number, optional) — Resolution in DPI, default `300`\n  - `format` (string, optional) — enum: all format keys. Override output format.\n  - `home_print` (boolean, optional) — Home printer mode: no bleed, no crop marks, content scaled to fit within safe margins, default `false`\n  - `safe_margin_mm` (number, optional) — Safe margin for home_print in mm, default `7`\n- Returns: text content (size/mode) + resource content (base64 PDF with `data:application/pdf;base64,...` URI)\n- Annotations: none\n\n---\n\n### Category: Metadata\n\n**`update_meta`**\n- Description: \"Update document metadata: design notes (your insights), team notes, and rating (0-5 stars). Use after composing or reviewing a design.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `designNotes` (string, optional) — Design insights, choices, and rationale\n  - `teamNotes` (string, optional) — Notes from team feedback or review\n  - `rating` (number, optional) — Quality rating 0-5 stars (validated: `min: 0, max: 5`)\n- Annotations: none\n\n---\n\n### Category: Layout Analysis\n\n**`check_layout`**\n- Description: \"Analyze layout for collisions, out-of-bounds elements, bleed zone violations, and irregular spacing. Returns a JSON diagnostic report. Use after composing or adjusting a layout.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `bleed_mm` (number, optional) — Bleed zone threshold in mm, default `5`\n  - `spacing_tolerance_mm` (number, optional) — Max deviation to consider spacing uniform, default `1`\n  - `size_tolerance_mm` (number, optional) — Max size difference to group similar elements, default `2`\n- Returns: `LayoutReport` JSON — see section 5\n- Annotations: readOnlyHint\n\n---\n\n### Category: UI Communication\n\n**`show_message`**\n- Description: \"Display a toast notification in the Illustrator UI. Use to inform the user about progress, results, or instructions.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `text` (string, required) — Message to display\n  - `level` (string, optional) — enum: `\"info\" | \"success\" | \"warning\"`, default `\"info\"`\n  - `duration` (number, optional) — Display duration in ms, default `3000`\n- Annotations: none\n\n---\n\n### Category: Client Store Debug (require browser at localhost:3333)\n\n**`inspect_store`**\n- Description: \"Read the client-side store state (phase, UI settings, selection, active doc). Requires a browser tab open at localhost:3333. Use to audit what the user sees and diagnose UI issues.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `slices` (string[], optional) — Which state slices to include. enum items: `\"phase\" | \"ui\" | \"doc\" | \"ephemeral\"`. Default: all.\n- Annotations: readOnlyHint\n\n**`dispatch_event`**\n- Description: \"Inject a typed event into the client-side store to simulate user interactions (select element, toggle UI, change phase). Requires a browser tab open at localhost:3333. Guards apply — invalid transitions are blocked.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `event_type` (string, required) — enum: `\"SELECT_ELEMENT\" | \"TOGGLE_SHOW_NAMES\" | \"TOGGLE_SHOW_BLEED\" | \"TOGGLE_SNAP\" | \"TOGGLE_PHOTO_PANEL\" | \"TOGGLE_DOC_COLLAPSE\" | \"TOGGLE_CAT_COLLAPSE\" | \"PHASE_TRANSITION\"`\n  - `id` (string, optional) — Element ID for SELECT_ELEMENT. Use null to deselect.\n  - `toggle` (boolean, optional) — For SELECT_ELEMENT: add/remove from multi-selection instead of replacing.\n  - `target` (string, optional) — Context for TOGGLE_DOC_COLLAPSE (docName), TOGGLE_CAT_COLLAPSE (category), or PHASE_TRANSITION (target phase: `idle | selected | editing_prop`).\n- Annotations: none\n\n**`get_event_log`**\n- Description: \"Read the client-side event log — recent dispatched events with timestamps, phases, and blocked status. Use to trace state transitions and debug guard blocks. Requires a browser tab open at localhost:3333.\"\n- Parameters:\n  - `limit` (number, optional) — Max entries to return, default `30`, max `200`\n  - `filter` (string, optional) — Substring filter on event type (e.g. `'DRAG'`, `'SELECT'`)\n  - `blocked_only` (boolean, optional) — Only show events that were blocked by guards\n- Annotations: readOnlyHint\n\n**Tool count: 36 total.**\n\n---\n\n## 2. Element Types (`src/types.ts`)\n\n### `BaseElement` (shared by all)\n```\nid: string\nname?: string\ntype: string\nopacity: number\nrotation: number\n```\n\n### `TextElement` (type: `\"text\"`)\nAdditional vs BaseElement:\n```\nx: number\ny: number\ntext: string\nfontSize: number\nfontFamily: string\nfontWeight: string\nfontStyle: string\nfill: string\ntextAnchor: string        -- \"start\" | \"middle\" | \"end\"\nmaxWidth: number | null\n```\n\n### `ImageElement` (type: `\"image\"`)\nAdditional vs BaseElement:\n```\nx: number\ny: number\nwidth: number\nheight: number\npath: string\nhref: string | null       -- base64 data URI (not persisted to DB)\npreserveAspectRatio: string\nnaturalWidth: number      -- source dimensions for crop math\nnaturalHeight: number\nobjectFit: \"cover\" | \"contain\" | \"fill\"\ncropX: number             -- 0-1, horizontal pan (0.5 = centered)\ncropY: number             -- 0-1, vertical pan (0.5 = centered)\ncropZoom: number          -- 1 = cover fit, >1 = extra zoom\nflipH: boolean\nflipV: boolean\nbrightness: number        -- percentage (100 = normal)\ncontrast: number          -- percentage (100 = normal)\ngrayscale: number         -- 0-100\nborderWidth: number\nborderColor: string\nborderRadius: number\nshadowX: number\nshadowY: number\nshadowBlur: number\nshadowColor: string\n```\n\n### `RectElement` (type: `\"rect\"`)\nAdditional vs BaseElement:\n```\nx: number\ny: number\nwidth: number\nheight: number\nfill: string\nstroke: string\nstrokeWidth: number\nrx: number               -- border radius\n```\n\n### `LineElement` (type: `\"line\"`)\nAdditional vs BaseElement:\n```\nx1: number\ny1: number\nx2: number\ny2: number\nstroke: string\nstrokeWidth: number\n```\n\n### `GroupElement` (type: `\"group\"`)\nAdditional vs BaseElement:\n```\nchildren: Element[]      -- recursive\n```\n\n### `Document`\n```\nname: string\ncategory: string\ncanvas: Canvas           -- { format, orientation, w, h, bg }\nmeta: DocMeta            -- { designNotes?, teamNotes?, rating? }\nelements: Element[]\nnextId: number\n```\n\n### `DocSummary` (listing)\n```\nname: string\ncategory: string\nformat: string\norientation: string\nrating: number\ncount: number\n```\n\n### `BBox` (internal)\n```\nx: number\ny: number\nw: number\nh: number\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Positioning Primitives (`src/positioning.ts`)\n\n### `resolvePosition(doc, type, args): ResolvedPos`\nComputes concrete x/y coordinates from relative positioning arguments. Returns `{ x?, y?, x1?, y1?, x2?, y2? }`.\n\n**Supported modes:**\n\n- **`below`** (string — element ID or name): Place below the reference. `y = ref.y + ref.h + gap`. For text, adds `fontSize * 0.85` baseline offset. Inherits `x` from reference element if no x/center_h.\n- **`above`** (string): Place above the reference. For text: `y = ref.y - gap`. For rect/image: `y = ref.y - gap - height`. For lines: offset by line height.\n- **`right_of`** (string): Place to the right. `x = ref.x + ref.w + gap`. Inherits `y` from reference if no y/center_v.\n- **`left_of`** (string): Place to the left. For text: accounts for `textAnchor` (`\"end\"` → `ref.x - gap`; `\"middle\"` → `ref.x - gap - w/2`; `\"start\"` → `ref.x - gap - w`). For rect/image: `ref.x - gap - width`.\n- **`center_h`** (boolean): Center horizontally on canvas. For `textAnchor: \"middle\"` → `canvas.w / 2`. For `\"end\"` → `canvas.w/2 + dims.w/2`. For `\"start\"` → `(canvas.w - dims.w) / 2`.\n- **`center_v`** (boolean): Center vertically on canvas. For text: `(canvas.h - dims.h)/2 + fontSize*0.85`.\n\nFor **lines**, `x1/y1/x2/y2` are treated as offsets from the resolved position.\n\n### `hasRelativeArgs(args): boolean`\nReturns `true` if any of `below | above | right_of | left_of | center_h | center_v` is set.\n\n### `computeAlign(doc, args): ElementDelta[]`\nReturns array of `{ id, props }` delta objects to apply. **AlignAxis** enum: `\"left\" | \"center_h\" | \"right\" | \"top\" | \"center_v\" | \"bottom\"`.\n\n- `left`: move all elements to minimum `bbox.x`\n- `right`: move all elements to maximum `bbox.x + bbox.w`\n- `center_h`: move all elements so their horizontal center aligns to the group's center\n- `top`: move all elements to minimum `bbox.y`\n- `bottom`: move all elements to maximum `bbox.y + bbox.h`\n- `center_v`: move all elements so their vertical center aligns to the group's center\n\nElements with delta < 0.01mm are skipped. Lines use `x1/y1/x2/y2` props; others use `x/y`.\n\n### `computeDistribute(doc, args): ElementDelta[]`\nDispatches to grid or linear distribution.\n\n**Linear (axis: `\"x\"` or `\"y\"`):**\n- Elements sorted by position on axis\n- If `gap` provided: fixed gap from first element's position\n- If no `gap`: uniform distribution across current extent (`gap = (extent - totalSize) / (n-1)`)\n\n**Grid (`grid` object provided):**\n- Calls `distributeGrid()` — places elements in `cols` columns\n- Uses `maxColW` and `maxRowH` for uniform cell sizing\n- `targetX = startX + col * (maxColW + col_gap)`\n- `targetY = startY + row * (maxRowH + row_gap)`\n\n### `distributeGrid(elements, grid): ElementDelta[]`\nParameters: `{ cols, col_gap, row_gap, start_x?, start_y? }`\n\n---\n\n## 4. SVG Rendering (`src/svg.ts`)\n\n### `buildSVG(embedImages: boolean = true, bleed_mm: number = 0): string`\nBuilds a complete SVG string from the active document.\n\n- ViewBox: `(-bleed, -bleed, totalW, totalH)` when bleed > 0, else `(0, 0, w, h)`\n- Background: `<rect>` covering the full viewBox with `canvas.bg`\n- Elements rendered depth-first (painter's algorithm, last = top)\n\n### Per-element SVG generation\n\n**`rect`**: `<rect x y width height fill stroke stroke-width rx opacity? transform?/>`\n\n**`line`**: `<line x1 y1 x2 y2 stroke stroke-width opacity? transform?/>`\n\n**`text`**:\n- Text wrapped via `wrapText()` if `maxWidth` is set, else split on `\\n`\n- `<text>` with `<tspan x dy>` for each line\n- Line height: `fontSize * 1.3`\n- `dy=\"0\"` for first tspan, `dy=lineHeight` for subsequent ones\n- Attributes: `font-family font-size font-weight font-style fill text-anchor opacity? transform?`\n\n**`image`** (three objectFit modes):\n- **`cover`** (default): Scales image to fill frame, crops via `<clipPath>`. Math: `baseScale = max(frameW/natW, frameH/natH)`, then `scale = baseScale * cropZoom`. `imgX = el.x - (imgW - frameW) * cropX`. `clipPath` id = `c_{el.id}`.\n- **`contain`**: `preserveAspectRatio=\"xMidYMid meet\"`, no clip path\n- **`fill`** (stretch): `preserveAspectRatio=\"none\"`, no clip path\n- **Flip transform**: `translate(cx,cy) scale(flipH,flipV) translate(-cx,-cy)` wrapped in `<g>`\n- **Border**: additional `<rect>` overlay with `fill=\"none\"` stroke\n- **Filters** (when brightness/contrast/grayscale != defaults):\n  - `<filter id=\"f_{el.id}\">` added to `<defs>`\n  - `<feColorMatrix type=\"saturate\" values=\"{1 - grayscale/100}\"/>`\n  - `<feComponentTransfer>` with `<feFuncR/G/B type=\"linear\" slope=\"{b*c}\" intercept=\"{(1-c)*0.5}\"/>`\n- **Shadow** (`shadowBlur > 0 || shadowX || shadowY`):\n  - `<feDropShadow dx dy stdDeviation flood-color flood-opacity=\"1\"/>`\n\n**`group`**: `<g id opacity? transform?>` with recursive children. Transform rotation computed from group bbox center: `rotate(rotation, cx, cy)`.\n\n**Image embedding**: when `embedImages=true`, uses `el.href` (base64 data URI). When false, uses `el.path` as file reference.\n\n---\n\n## 5. Layout Analysis (`src/layout.ts`)\n\n### `bbox(el: Element): BBox`\nComputes bounding box per element type:\n- `rect`, `image`: `{ x, y, w: width, h: height }`\n- `line`: `{ x: min(x1,x2), y: min(y1,y2), w: |x2-x1| || 0.5, h: |y2-y1| || 0.5 }`\n- `text`: Uses `wrapText()` or `\\n` split for line count. Width: measured via `measureTextWidth()` if `maxWidth`, else `lineLen * fontSize * 0.55`. Height: `fontSize * lineCount * 1.3`. Adjusts `x` for `textAnchor`: `\"middle\"` → `x - w/2`, `\"end\"` → `x - w`. `y` adjusted: `y - fontSize * 0.85` (top of text box).\n- `group`: Union of all children bboxes (recursive)\n\n### `checkLayout(d, bleed, spaceTol, sizeTol): LayoutReport`\n\n**`LayoutReport` shape:**\n```\nstructuralLayers: string[]      -- IDs of elements covering >50% canvas area\noverlaps: Array<{\n  a, b: string,\n  a_type, b_type: string,\n  intersection: { x, y, w, h },\n  area_mm2: number\n}>\noutOfBounds: Array<{\n  id: string,\n  side: \"left\" | \"top\" | \"right\" | \"bottom\",\n  overflow_mm: number\n}>\nbleedZone: Array<{\n  id: string,\n  side: string,\n  distance_mm: number\n}>\nspacingGroups: Array<{\n  ids: string[],\n  type: string,\n  axis: \"horizontal\" | \"vertical\",\n  gaps_mm: number[],\n  avg_gap_mm: number,\n  uniform: boolean\n}>\ncolorWarnings: Array<{\n  id, type, property, value, reason: string\n}>\n```\n\n**Checks performed:**\n1. **Structural layer detection**: elements with area > 50% of canvas, or semi-transparent rects spanning 95% width/height — excluded from overlap detection\n2. **Pairwise overlap detection**: axis-aligned bounding box intersection test on all non-structural leaf elements, reports intersection rectangle and area\n3. **Out-of-bounds**: any element with bbox extending outside canvas (x<0, y<0, x+w>cW, y+h>cH)\n4. **Bleed zone violations**: elements whose edges are within `bleed` mm of canvas border but NOT full-bleed (< 95% canvas size)\n5. **Spacing group detection**: groups of 3+ elements with same type and similar size (within `sizeTol`), checks if gaps are uniform within `spaceTol` mm\n6. **CMYK color warnings**: detects rgba/hsla colors with alpha, pure black `#000000`, and fully saturated colors (max channel = 255, min = 0) on `fill`, `stroke`, `borderColor`, `shadowColor` properties\n\n---\n\n## 6. Font Measurement (`src/fonts.ts`)\n\n### Available fonts (loaded via opentype.js):\n\n| Family | Weight | Style | File |\n|--------|--------|-------|------|\n| Libre Baskerville | normal | normal | `LibreBaskerville[wght].ttf` |\n| Libre Baskerville | bold | normal | `LibreBaskerville[wght].ttf` |\n| Libre Baskerville | normal | italic | `LibreBaskerville-Italic[wght].ttf` |\n| Libre Baskerville | bold | italic | `LibreBaskerville-Italic[wght].ttf` |\n| Source Sans 3 | normal | normal | `SourceSans3[wght].ttf` |\n| Source Sans 3 | 300 | normal | `SourceSans3[wght].ttf` |\n| Source Sans 3 | 600 | normal | `SourceSans3[wght].ttf` |\n| Source Sans 3 | bold | normal | `SourceSans3[wght].ttf` |\n| Source Sans 3 | 700 | normal | `SourceSans3[wght].ttf` |\n| Source Sans 3 | normal | italic | `SourceSans3-Italic[wght].ttf` |\n\nFont map key: `\"{family}|{weight}|{style}\"`. Falls back to first loaded font if key not found. Falls back to `text.length * fontSize * 0.55` if no font loaded.\n\n### `loadFonts(): void`\nLoads all fonts from `FONTS_DIR` into `fontMap`. Uses a file-level cache (`fileCache`) to avoid re-reading same `.ttf` files.\n\n### `getFont(fontFamily?, fontWeight?, fontStyle?): opentype.Font | null`\nLooks up font by key. Falls back to first available font.\n\n### `measureTextWidth(text, fontSize, fontFamily?, fontWeight?, fontStyle?): number`\nReturns advance width in mm using `font.getAdvanceWidth(text, fontSize)`.\n\n### `wrapText(text, maxWidth, fontSize, fontFamily?, fontWeight?, fontStyle?): string[]`\nReturns array of wrapped lines.\n- If `maxWidth` is null/0: splits only on `\\n` (one array entry per paragraph line)\n- Splits text into paragraphs on `\\n`, then greedily wraps words within each paragraph\n- Word boundary: whitespace; empty words are filtered\n- Greedy algorithm: builds line word by word, breaks when `measureTextWidth(test) > maxWidth`\n\n---\n\n## 7. Tree Operations (`src/tree.ts`)\n\nAll functions operate on `Element[]` trees with recursive group descent.\n\n### `findInTree(elements, idOrName): Element | undefined`\nDepth-first search by `el.id === idOrName || el.name === idOrName`. Recurses into group children.\n\n### `findInTreeWithParent(elements, idOrName): FindResult | undefined`\nReturns `{ element, parent: Element[], index }` — the parent array and index needed for splice operations.\n\n### `flattenLeaves(elements): Element[]`\nReturns all leaf elements (non-group), depth-first. Groups themselves are excluded, only their leaf descendants are included.\n\n### `reassignIds(elements, startId): number`\nRecursively assigns new sequential IDs (`e{n}`) to all elements. Returns updated `nextId` counter. Used after duplication to avoid ID collisions.\n\n### `countElements(elements): number`\nCounts all elements recursively including group containers themselves.\n\n### `insertIntoGroup(elements, newEl, groupId?): boolean`\nIf `groupId` is null/undefined: pushes to top-level array, returns `true`. Otherwise: finds group by ID/name, pushes to `group.children`, returns `true`. Returns `false` if group not found.\n\n### `isAncestorOf(elements, ancestorId, targetId): boolean`\nReturns `true` if `ancestorId === targetId` OR if the element named `ancestorId` is a group containing `targetId` in its descendants. Used to prevent cycles in `add_to_group`.\n\n---\n\n## 8. Document Operations (`src/documents.ts`)\n\n### Module-scoped state\n- `documents: Map<string, Document>` — in-memory document store\n- `activeDocName: string | null`\n- `selectedElementId: string | null`\n- `selectedAsset: string | null`\n- `clients: Set<WebSocket>` — connected browser clients\n- `AUTO_SAVE_DELAY = 2000` ms debounce\n- `dirtyDocs: Set<string>` — names of modified documents pending save\n\n### Accessors (all exported)\n- `getActiveDoc(): Document | null`\n- `getDocuments(): Map<string, Document>`\n- `getClients(): Set<WebSocket>`\n- `getActiveDocName(): string | null`\n- `getSelectedElementId(): string | null`\n- `getSelectedAsset(): string | null`\n\n### Mutators\n- `setActiveDoc(name: string | null): void`\n- `setSelectedElementId(id: string | null): void`\n- `setSelectedAsset(file: string | null): void`\n- `addClient(ws: WebSocket): void`\n- `removeClient(ws: WebSocket): void`\n- `genId(): string` — returns `\"el_{d.nextId++}\"` (note: `handlers.ts` uses `\"e{nextId++}\"` — minor inconsistency)\n\n### Persistence\n- `getStore(): DocumentStore`\n- `saveDocToDisk(d: Document): string` — calls `store.saveDoc(d)`, returns `\"db:{name}\"`\n- `loadAllDocuments(): void` — initializes `DocumentStore`, migrates from JSON if DB empty, loads all docs, sets `activeDocName` to most recently updated\n- `markDirty(name?): void` — adds to `dirtyDocs`, debounces `flushDirty()` at 2s\n- `flushAll(): void` — flushes immediately + closes DB (called on SIGINT/SIGTERM)\n- `deleteDocument(name: string): void` — removes from DB + memory map\n\n### Listings\n- `getDocList(): DocSummary[]`\n- `listAssets(): string[]` — scans `ASSETS_DIR` recursively for `.png | .jpg | .jpeg | .svg | .webp | .gif`\n\n---\n\n## 9. Export Formats\n\n### SVG (`src/svg.ts`)\n- Function: `buildSVG(embedImages = true, bleed_mm = 0): string`\n- Options: image embedding toggle, bleed margin expansion\n- Used by: `export_svg` tool, `snapshot` tool, `export_pdf` (SVG as intermediate), `/api/export-svg` HTTP endpoint\n\n### PDF (`src/pdf.ts`)\n- Function: `generatePdf(opts: PdfOptions): Promise<Uint8Array>`\n- Pipeline: SVG → inject crop marks → wrap in HTML with embedded `@font-face` → headless Chrome (puppeteer-core) → PDF binary\n\n**PdfOptions:**\n```\nbleed_mm?: number      -- default 3, ignored in home_print\ncrop_marks?: boolean   -- default true, ignored in home_print\ndpi?: number           -- default 300\nformat?: string        -- override canvas format\nhome_print?: boolean   -- default false\nsafe_margin_mm?: number -- default 7 (home_print only)\n```\n\n**Two modes:**\n- **Pro print**: `@page { size: {totalW}mm {totalH}mm; margin: 0 }`. SVG rendered at exact bleed dimensions. Crop marks injected as SVG `<line>` elements (8 lines at 4 corners, 5mm length, 1mm offset from trim edge, 0.15mm stroke).\n- **Home print**: `@page { size: {contentW}mm {contentH}mm; margin: 0 }`. SVG scaled down by `min(printableW/contentW, printableH/contentH)` and centered via CSS `margin`.\n\nChrome detection: checks macOS/Linux candidate paths, falls back to `CHROME_PATH` env var.\n\n### DOCX (`src/docx.ts`)\n- Function: `generateDocx(): Promise<Uint8Array>`\n- Not exposed as a tool — only via `/api/export-docx` HTTP endpoint\n- Tailored specifically for political flyer/brochure layout (hardcoded palette, spatial heuristics)\n- Pipeline:\n  1. Flatten all elements to leaves, sort by Y position\n  2. Detect gold accent color from rect/text fills via regex\n  3. Categorize texts by Y position relative to detected zones: heroTexts, introTexts, progTitle, axeTexts (cards), footerTexts\n  4. Build docx using `docx` library: ImageRun (hero), Paragraphs, Tables (2-column axes grid), gold horizontal rules\n  5. `Packer.toBuffer()` → `Uint8Array`\n\n**Palette constants:**\n```\nVERT = \"2B3D35\"\nGRIS = \"3E3E3E\"\nCREAM = \"FDFBF7\"\nWHITE = \"FFFFFF\"\nHERO_BG = \"1A2B22\"\n```\n\n### PNG snapshot (`index.ts` handlers)\n- Uses `@resvg/resvg-js` (Rust-based Resvg) to render SVG to PNG\n- Loads all `.ttf` files from `FONTS_DIR` into Resvg font buffer\n- `fitTo: { mode: \"width\", value: w }` — default width 1200px, aspect ratio preserved\n- Returns base64-encoded PNG as MCP image content\n\n---\n\n## 10. Canvas Format Presets (`src/types.ts`)\n\n```\nFORMATS = {\n  A2: { w: 420, h: 594 },     -- mm\n  A3: { w: 297, h: 420 },\n  A4: { w: 210, h: 297 },\n  A5: { w: 148, h: 210 },\n  HD: { w: 480, h: 270 },     -- screen (mm-equivalent)\n  MACBOOK: { w: 457, h: 286 },\n  IPAD: { w: 341, h: 256 },\n  MOBILE: { w: 135, h: 270 },\n}\n\nSCREEN_FORMATS = Set([\"HD\", \"MACBOOK\", \"IPAD\", \"MOBILE\"])\n```\n\nScreen formats ignore `orientation` flag (portrait/paysage has no effect). Paper formats swap `w`/`h` when `orientation === \"paysage\"`.\n\n---\n\n## 11. Client-Side Primitives (`client/`)\n\n### AppEvent Types (`client/store/events.ts`)\n\nAll events in the `AppEvent` discriminated union:\n\n**`DocEvent`:**\n- `SERVER_STATE` — `{ doc: Document | null, docList: DocSummary[] }` — full server state replacement\n\n**`UIEvent`:**\n- `SELECT_ELEMENT` — `{ id: string | null, toggle?: boolean }`\n- `TOGGLE_LAYERS_PANEL` — no payload\n- `TOGGLE_PROPS_PANEL` — no payload\n- `TOGGLE_PHOTO_PANEL` — no payload\n- `SET_PHOTO_SAVED_H` — `{ height: number }`\n- `TOGGLE_SHOW_NAMES` — no payload\n- `TOGGLE_SHOW_BLEED` — no payload\n- `TOGGLE_SNAP` — no payload\n- `TOGGLE_LOCK_DOC` — no payload\n- `SET_ASSETS` — `{ assets: AssetsData }`\n\n**`EphemeralEvent`:**\n- `DRAG_START` — `{ elId: string }`\n- `DRAG_MOVE` — `{ snapGuides: Guide[] }`\n- `DRAG_END` — no payload\n- `SET_ZOOM_LEVEL` — `{ level: number }`\n\n**`RefEvent`:**\n- `SET_WS` — `{ ws: WebSocket | null }`\n- `SET_ZOOM_BEHAVIOR` — `{ behavior: any }` (d3-zoom behavior)\n- `SET_LAST_FIT_KEY` — `{ key: string | null }`\n\n**`PhaseEvent`:**\n- `PHASE_TRANSITION` — `{ to: AppPhase }`\n\n---\n\n### Phase State Machine (`client/store/guards.ts` + `client/store/reducers.ts`)\n\n**`AppPhase` type:** `\"loading\" | \"idle\" | \"selected\" | \"dragging\" | \"editing_prop\" | \"loading_doc\"`\n\n**Phase transitions (from `phaseReducer`):**\n- `PHASE_TRANSITION { to }` → any target phase (always allowed)\n- `SERVER_STATE` with doc received: `\"loading\" | \"loading_doc\"` → `\"selected\"` (if selectedIds > 0) or `\"idle\"`\n- `SERVER_STATE` with doc=null: any → `\"loading\"`\n- `SELECT_ELEMENT`: → `\"selected\"` (if selection non-empty) or `\"idle\"` (if empty); blocked during `\"dragging\"`\n- `DRAG_START`: `\"selected\"` → `\"dragging\"`\n- `DRAG_END`: `\"dragging\"` → `\"selected\"`\n\n**Guard middleware table** (`client/store/guards.ts`):\nEvents allowed by phase:\n\n| Event | Allowed phases |\n|-------|---------------|\n| `SERVER_STATE`, `SET_WS`, `SET_ZOOM_BEHAVIOR`, `SET_LAST_FIT_KEY`, `PHASE_TRANSITION` | `*` (all phases) |\n| `SELECT_ELEMENT` | loading, idle, selected, editing_prop, loading_doc |\n| `DRAG_START` | selected only |\n| `DRAG_MOVE` | dragging only |\n| `DRAG_END` | dragging only |\n| `TOGGLE_DOC_COLLAPSE`, `TOGGLE_CAT_COLLAPSE`, `TOGGLE_PHOTO_PANEL`, `SET_PHOTO_SAVED_H`, `TOGGLE_SHOW_NAMES`, `TOGGLE_SHOW_BLEED`, `TOGGLE_SNAP`, `SET_ASSETS` | `*` (all phases) |\n\nNote: `TOGGLE_LAYERS_PANEL`, `TOGGLE_PROPS_PANEL`, `TOGGLE_LOCK_DOC` have no guard rule — they pass through unconditionally (rule === undefined → pass).\n\nBlocked events are logged to the event log with `blocked: true` but do NOT throw errors.\n\n---\n\n### Snap System (`client/snap.ts`)\n\n**Constants:**\n- `THRESHOLD = 2` mm — snap activation distance\n\n**Types:**\n- `Guide: { axis: \"h\" | \"v\", pos: number }` — snap guide line to render\n- `SnapResult: { x, y, guides: Guide[] }` — corrected position + visual guides\n- `SnapTargets: { xSnaps: number[], ySnaps: number[] }` — pre-computed snap positions\n\n**`collectSnapTargets(elements, excludeIds, canvas): SnapTargets`**\n- Canvas snaps: `[0, canvas.w/2, canvas.w]` (x) and `[0, canvas.h/2, canvas.h]` (y)\n- Element snaps: for each non-excluded leaf element: left edge, center, right edge (x); top, center, bottom (y)\n- Bbox computed inline (same formula as `src/layout.ts:bbox`)\n\n**`computeSnap(dragBbox, targets): SnapResult`**\nFor each axis independently:\n- Tests all snap targets against 3 anchors of the dragged element (left/center/right for x; top/center/bottom for y)\n- Selects closest snap within `THRESHOLD`\n- Returns corrected position and active guide lines\n- If snap found: returns `{ axis: \"v\", pos: guideX }` or `{ axis: \"h\", pos: guideY }`\n\n---\n\n### Image Editor (`client/image-editor.ts`)\n\n**Exported functions:**\n- `openImageEditor(elId: string): void` — Opens overlay, loads element data, builds preview and controls. Triggered via `document.addEventListener('open-image-editor', ...)` custom event.\n- `closeImageEditor(apply = false): void` — Closes overlay. If `apply=true`: sends update to server via `sendUpdate()` and pushes undo entry via `undoManager.push()`.\n- `initImageEditor(): void` — Wires all event listeners (close/apply/cancel buttons, escape key, backdrop click).\n\n**Editable properties (draft state):**\n- `objectFit: 'cover' | 'contain' | 'fill'`\n- `cropX: number` — 0-1 horizontal pan\n- `cropY: number` — 0-1 vertical pan\n- `cropZoom: number` — 1-5, default 1\n- `flipH: boolean`\n- `flipV: boolean`\n- `brightness: number` — 50-150\n- `contrast: number` — 50-150\n- `grayscale: number` — 0-100\n\n**Interaction:**\n- Drag pan: mouse drag on preview frame updates `cropX/cropY` — pixel delta converted to crop fraction using excess image area math\n- Wheel zoom: `+/-0.05` per wheel event, clamped `1-5`\n- Zoom slider: `1-5`, step `0.1`\n- Brightness slider: `50-150`, step `1`\n- Contrast slider: `50-150`, step `1`\n- Grayscale slider: `0-100`, step `1`\n- Flip buttons: toggle `flipH/flipV`\n- Reset: restores all defaults (`objectFit: cover, cropX/Y: 0.5, cropZoom: 1, flipH/V: false, brightness/contrast: 100, grayscale: 0`)\n\n---\n\n### Store Architecture (`client/store/`)\n\n**`AppState` shape:**\n```\ndoc:       DocumentSlice   -- currentDoc, docList\nui:        UISlice         -- selectedIds[], panel collapse states, showNames/Bleed/snap/lock, assetsData\nephemeral: EphemeralSlice  -- snapGuides[], zoomLevel\nrefs:      RefsSlice       -- ws, zoomBehavior, lastFitKey\nphase:     AppPhase\n```\n\n**`Store` class (`store.ts`):**\n- `state: AppState` (read-only getter)\n- `dispatch(event: AppEvent): void` — runs middlewares in order (return `null` = block), applies `rootReducer`, notifies listeners\n- `subscribe(listener: Listener): () => void` — returns unsubscribe function\n- `use(middleware: Middleware): void`\n- Initial state: `phase: \"loading\"`, all panels uncollapsed except photo, `showNames: true`, `showBleed: true`, `snapEnabled: true`\n\n**Middleware type:** `(state: AppState, event: AppEvent) => AppEvent | null`\n\n**Listener type:** `(state: AppState, prevState: AppState, event: AppEvent) => void`\n\n**`rootReducer`:** Delegates to 5 pure slice reducers (`docReducer`, `uiReducer`, `ephemeralReducer`, `refsReducer`, `phaseReducer`). Returns same reference if nothing changed (enables `===` equality checks in subscribers).\n\n---\n\n### Bus Events (`src/bus.ts`)\n\nServer-side typed event bus (`BusEvents`):\n- `\"document:created\"` — `{ name }`\n- `\"document:saved\"` — `{ name }`\n- `\"document:loaded\"` — `{ name }`\n- `\"document:deleted\"` — `{ name }`\n- `\"canvas:changed\"` — `{}`\n- `\"element:added\"` — `{ id }`\n- `\"element:updated\"` — `{ id }` (id = `\"batch\"` for multi-updates)\n- `\"element:deleted\"` — `{ id }`\n- `\"element:reordered\"` — `{ id, action }`\n- `\"elements:cleared\"` — `{}`\n- `\"meta:updated\"` — `{}`\n- `\"toast\"` — `{ text, level?, duration? }`\n\nMutation events broadcast full state via WebSocket to all connected clients. Toast events broadcast toast message only.\n\n---\n\n### WebSocket Protocol (server → client and client → server)\n\n**Server → Client:**\n- `{ type: \"state\", doc: Document | null, docList: DocSummary[] }` — full state push (on any mutation)\n- `{ type: \"toast\", text, level, duration }` — toast notification\n- `{ type: \"reload\" }` — live reload trigger (dev only, watches `public/`)\n- `{ type: \"*_response\", _reqId, ...data }` — responses to `inspect_request`, `dispatch_request`, `log_request`\n\n**Client → Server (WebSocket messages):**\n- `{ type: \"load_document\", name }`\n- `{ type: \"select_element\", id }` — sets `selectedElementId`\n- `{ type: \"select_asset\", file }`\n- `{ type: \"update_element\", id, props }`\n- `{ type: \"batch_update\", updates: [{id, props}] }`\n- `{ type: \"delete_element\", id }`\n- `{ type: \"reorder_element\", id, action }`\n- `{ type: \"save_document\" }`\n- `{ type: \"update_canvas\", format?, orientation?, bg? }`\n- `{ type: \"update_meta\", designNotes?, teamNotes?, rating? }`\n- `{ type: \"add_element\", element }` — element must have `type`; ID assigned server-side\n- `{ type: \"paste_elements\", elements[] }` — IDs assigned server-side\n- `{ type: \"clear_canvas\" }`\n- `{ type: \"delete_document\", name }`\n- `{ type: \"inspect_response\", _reqId, ...sliceData }` — response to inspect_request\n- `{ type: \"dispatch_response\", _reqId, phase, selectedIds }` — response to dispatch_request\n- `{ type: \"log_response\", _reqId, entries }` — response to log_request\n\n---\n\n### HTTP API Endpoints (`index.ts`)\n\n- `GET /` — Serves `public/index.html` with `{{TITLE}}` / `{{SUBTITLE}}` injection (from `APP_TITLE`/`APP_SUBTITLE` env vars)\n- `GET /assets/*` — Static file serving from `ASSETS_DIR`\n- `GET /api/assets` — Returns `{ images: [{file, title, ...}] }` from `metadata.json` or auto-generated list\n- `POST /api/upload` — Body: `{ filename: string, data: string (base64) }`, limit 50mb. Saves to `ASSETS_DIR`, updates `metadata.json` if present.\n- `GET /api/export-svg?embed=true|false` — SVG download with `Content-Disposition`\n- `GET /api/export-docx` — DOCX download\n- `GET /api/export-pdf?home_print=&bleed=&crop_marks=&dpi=&safe_margin=` — PDF download\n\n---\n\n### Persistence Layer (`src/store.ts` — `DocumentStore`)\n\n**SQLite schema (bun:sqlite, WAL mode, schema version 1):**\n```sql\nCREATE TABLE documents (\n  name       TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n  category   TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'general',\n  canvas     TEXT NOT NULL,        -- JSON\n  meta       TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}',  -- JSON\n  elements   TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT '[]',  -- JSON (href stripped)\n  next_id    INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,\n  created_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now')),\n  updated_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now'))\n);\n```\n\n**CRUD methods:**\n- `saveDoc(d: Document): void` — UPSERT\n- `saveDocs(docs: Document[]): void` — transaction\n- `loadAll(): Document[]` — ORDER BY updated_at ASC (last = newest)\n- `loadOne(name: string): Document | null`\n- `deleteDoc(name: string): void`\n- `isEmpty(): boolean`\n- `migrateFromJson(): Document[]` — reads `documents/*.json`, imports to SQLite\n- `close(): void`\n\n**`href` stripping**: `stripElements()` removes `href` from images before persisting (base64 is re-hydrated on load from `el.path`). `hydrateImages()` re-adds `href` from `loadImageAsDataUri()` after loading.\n\n---\n\n### Config (`src/config.ts`)\n\nAll constants are path-based, derived from `__dirname`:\n- `MODULE_DIR` — directory of `src/`\n- `PROJECT_ROOT` — parent of `src/` (= repo root)\n- `ASSETS_DIR` — `{PROJECT_ROOT}/assets`\n- `DOCS_DIR` — `{MODULE_DIR}/documents` (legacy JSON, auto-created)\n- `FONTS_DIR` — `{MODULE_DIR}/fonts`\n- `DB_PATH` — `{MODULE_DIR}/documents.db` or `$ILLUSTRATOR_DB`\n- `APP_TITLE` — `\"MCP Illustrator\"` or `$ILLUSTRATOR_TITLE`\n- `APP_SUBTITLE` — `\"\"` or `$ILLUSTRATOR_SUBTITLE`\n\n---\n\n## Essential
